<h1 align="center">CSS Bangla Documentation</h1>

- ## CSS ‡¶ï‡¶ø?
    
    CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ Full Meaning ‚Äú**Cascading Style Sheets**‚Äù. ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü HTML Or XML Document ‡¶è‡¶∞ Presentation ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Formatting ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ Layout, Colors, Fonts ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Animations ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø Control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Individual HTML Element ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ Group of HTML Element ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá Style ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ CSS Associating Style Rules ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá Selectors ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá HTML Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ Style Provide ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ  Selectors ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® HTML Element ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Heading, Paragraph ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ Class Assigned ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Style Properties ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Apply ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Multiple Web Pages Layout ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá Control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ CSS Cascading Hierarchy  ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Element ‡¶è Multiple Style Rules Apply ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Browser ‡¶è‡¶á Rules ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Final Style Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ 
    
    ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ HTML Use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Website ‡¶è‡¶∞ Structure ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ CSS Use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Creative and Dynamic Webpage design ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ 
    
    CSS3 ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Latest Version. ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ö‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ 
    
- ## CSS ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨?
    
    CSS ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ HTML ‡¶°‡¶ï‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá CSS ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶â‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:
    
    - CSS ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá HTML ‡¶°‡¶ï‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Text, Button, Image, Link ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∞ Style (color, font-family, font-size, font-weight, margin, padding etc.) ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø HTML ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ Content ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ CSS ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á Content ‡¶è‡¶∞  Design ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
    - ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á CSS ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶™‡ßÉ‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶†‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶É‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§
    - CSS ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá Webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ Loading Speed ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£, CSS Code ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ Browser ‡¶è Load ‡¶π‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞, ‡¶§‡¶æ Website ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ì‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶™ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
    - CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® Browser ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Device ‡¶è Website ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ú‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®, Responsive Design ‡¶¨‡¶æ Media Query ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Mobile, Tablet, Desktop ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø Device ‡¶è Website ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡•§
    - CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡ßá Website ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá Navigate(‡¶è‡¶ï webpage ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï webpage ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ) ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ Text Contrast ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã, ‡¶¨‡¶æ Font-Size ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßÉ‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß‡ßÄ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßü‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßú‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
    - CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ Visual Effects ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Hover Effect, Transition, Animation ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Website ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì Attractive ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Interactive ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§
    - CSS ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá Code ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá HTML ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Styling ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Code ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶†‡¶®‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá CSS Code ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ File ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá HTML File ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Code ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶†‡¶®‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡•§
    - ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶®‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ Design ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨ CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® Theme ‡¶¨‡¶æ Layout ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
    
    ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá, CSS ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßü‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ 
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® HTML ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Web Page ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ Webpage ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ Content ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Style ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html lang="en">
      <head>
        <meta charset="UTF-8" />
        <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
        <title>Home</title>
      </head>
      <body>
        <!-- ========== Start Header Section ========== -->
        <header>
          <div>
            <div>
              <h2><a href="#">Logo</a></h2>
            </div>
            <nav>
              <li><a href="#">Home</a></li>
              <li><a href="#">About</a></li>
              <li><a href="#">Services</a></li>
              <li><a href="#">Blog</a></li>
              <li><a href="#">Contact</a></li>
            </nav>
          </div>
        </header>
        <!-- ========== End Header Section ========== -->
    
        <!-- ========== Start Hero Section ========== -->
        <main>
          <div>
            <!-- hero left side start -->
            <div>
              <div>
                <p>Pro.Beyond</p>
                <p>IPhone 14 <span>Pro</span></p>
              </div>
              <p>Created to change everything for the better. For everyone</p>
              <div>
                <button>Shop Now</button>
              </div>
            </div>
            <!-- hero left side end -->
            <!-- hero right side start -->
            <div>
              <img
                src="https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1678533511793-3e4098b854e0?q=80&w=1470&auto=format&fit=crop&ixlib=rb-4.0.3&ixid=M3wxMjA3fDB8MHxwaG90by1wYWdlfHx8fGVufDB8fHx8fA%3D%3D"
                alt="Iphone 14 pro"
              />
            </div>
            <!-- hero right side end -->
          </div>
        </main>
        <!-- ========== End Hero Section ========== -->
    
        <!-- ========== Start footer Section ========== -->
        <footer>
          <p>&copy; Copyright 2024</p>
        </footer>
        <!-- ========== End footer Section ========== -->
      </body>
    </html>
    
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ Webpage ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ó‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶∑‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡ßÄ‡ßü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶¨ ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá CSS. CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ Example ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Design ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá Look ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡¶É
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html lang="en">
      <head>
        <meta charset="UTF-8" />
        <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
        <title>Home</title>
        <style>
          * {
            margin: 0;
            padding: 0;
            box-sizing: border-box;
          }
    
          /* basic */
          body {
            font-family: "Segoe UI", Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif;
          }
    
          a {
            text-decoration: none;
          }
    
          li {
            list-style: none;
          }
    
          /* reusable code */
          .container {
            max-width: 1140px;
            height: auto;
            margin: auto;
            height: inherit;
          }
    
          /* header section */
          header {
            height: 70px;
            width: 100%;
            background: lightseagreen;
            box-shadow: 0 2px 5px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.16),
              0 2px 10px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.12);
          }
    
          header .container {
            display: flex;
            height: 70px;
            justify-content: space-between;
            align-items: center;
          }
    
          .logo a {
            font-size: 24px;
            line-height: 30px;
            color: white;
          }
    
          nav {
            display: flex;
            justify-content: center;
            align-items: center;
            gap: 12px;
          }
    
          nav li {
            padding: 0px 12px;
            border-radius: 5px;
            transition: all 0.2s ease-in-out;
          }
          nav li:hover {
            & a {
              color: black;
            }
          }
    
          nav li a {
            color: white;
            font-size: 20px;
          }
    
          .active {
            color: black;
          }
    
          /* main Section  */
          main {
            height: 500px;
            width: 100%;
            background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #654ea3, #daafc8);
          }
    
          main .container {
            display: flex;
            align-items: center;
            gap: 10px;
          }
    
          main .hero-left {
            flex-basis: 50%;
          }
          main .hero-right {
            flex-basis: 50%;
            height: 80%;
          }
    
          .hero-img {
            height: 100%;
            width: 100%;
          }
    
          .hero-title {
            display: flex;
            flex-direction: column;
            gap: 8px;
          }
    
          .hero-title .small-title {
            color: white;
            font-size: 20px;
            font-weight: 600;
          }
    
          .hero-title .big-title {
            color: white;
            font-size: 90px;
            font-weight: 100;
            & span {
              font-weight: 600;
            }
          }
    
          .hero-description {
            color: white;
            font-size: 18px;
            font-weight: 500;
          }
    
          .hero-btn {
            height: 56px;
            width: 181px;
            margin-top: 16px;
            font-size: 16px;
            font-weight: 600;
            background: transparent;
            color: white;
            border: 1px solid #ddd;
            border-radius: 8px;
            transition: all 300ms ease-in-out;
            outline: none;
            &:hover {
              background: #eeccff;
              color: #1a1a1a;
              border: 1px solid #dd99ff;
            }
          }
    
          /* footer section */
          footer {
            width: 100%;
            height: 60px;
            background: lightseagreen;
            display: flex;
            justify-content: center;
            align-items: center;
          }
          footer p {
            font-size: 18px;
            font-weight: 600;
          }
    
          /* responsive design */
          @media (max-width: 1140px) {
            .container {
              padding: 0 12px;
            }
          }
    
          /* responsive for tablet devices */
          @media (max-width: 767px) {
            .container {
              padding: 0 12px;
            }
    
            /* main section */
            main {
              height: auto;
            }
            main .container {
              padding-top: 50px;
              flex-direction: column;
            }
            .hero-title {
              align-items: center;
            }
    
            .hero-title .big-title {
              font-size: 75px;
              text-align: center;
            }
    
            .hero-description {
              text-align: center;
            }
    
            .hero-btn-div {
              display: flex;
              justify-content: center;
            }
    
            .hero-right {
              text-align: center;
            }
    
            .hero-img {
              width: 70%;
            }
          }
    
          /* responsive for mobile device */
          @media (max-width: 640px) {
            nav {
              display: flex;
              justify-content: end;
              align-items: center;
              gap: 0px;
            }
    
            nav li {
              padding: 8px 8px;
            }
    
            nav li a {
              font-size: 14px;
            }
    
            /* main section */
            .hero-img {
              width: 100%;
            }
    
            /* footer section */
            footer p {
              font-size: 14px;
            }
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <!-- ========== Start Header Section ========== -->
        <header>
          <div class="container">
            <div>
              <h2 class="logo"><a href="#">Logo</a></h2>
            </div>
            <nav>
              <li><a href="#" class="active">Home</a></li>
              <li><a href="#">About</a></li>
              <li><a href="#">Services</a></li>
              <li><a href="#">Contact</a></li>
            </nav>
          </div>
        </header>
        <!-- ========== End Header Section ========== -->
    
        <!-- ========== Start Hero Section ========== -->
        <main>
          <div class="container">
            <!-- hero left side start -->
            <div class="hero-left">
              <div class="hero-title">
                <p class="small-title">Pro.Beyond</p>
                <p class="big-title">IPhone 14 <span>Pro</span></p>
              </div>
              <p class="hero-description">
                Created to change everything for the better. For everyone
              </p>
              <div class="hero-btn-div">
                <button class="hero-btn">Shop Now</button>
              </div>
            </div>
            <!-- hero left side end -->
            <!-- hero right side start -->
            <div class="hero-right">
              <img
                src="https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1678533511793-3e4098b854e0?q=80&w=1470&auto=format&fit=crop&ixlib=rb-4.0.3&ixid=M3wxMjA3fDB8MHxwaG90by1wYWdlfHx8fGVufDB8fHx8fA%3D%3D"
                alt="iphone 14 pro"
                class="hero-img"
              />
            </div>
            <!-- hero right side end -->
          </div>
        </main>
        <!-- ========== End Hero Section ========== -->
    
        <!-- ========== Start footer Section ========== -->
        <footer>
          <p>&copy; Copyright 2024</p>
        </footer>
        <!-- ========== End footer Section ========== -->
      </body>
    </html>
    
    ```
    
    ---
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á CSS Syntax ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü?
    
    CSS Syntax:
    
    ![https://www.w3schools.com/css/img_selector.gif](https://www.w3schools.com/css/img_selector.gif)
    
    CSS ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶á Syntax ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá Code ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Selector Point ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá HTML Element ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ HTML ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á Element ‡¶ï‡ßá Style ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á Selector ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Selector ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® HTML Tag ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ CSS Class ‡¶¨‡¶æ CSS Id ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá Declaration Block. ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï Declaration Block ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Syntax ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø  Declaration Block Semicolon(;) ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø Declaration Block ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ Property Name ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Property Value. ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã colon(:) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Separate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```css
    p {
      color: red;
      text-align: center;
    }
    ```
    
    - ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **`p`**   ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá CSS Selector. (‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá HTML Element ‡¶ï‡ßá Style ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§)
    - **`color`** ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Property Name. ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ **`red`** ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Property Value.
    - **`text-align`** ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Property Name. ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ **`center`** ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Property Value.
    
    ---
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á CSS Selectors ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
    
    CSS Selectors ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü HTML Element ‡¶ï‡ßá Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Style ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ CSS Rule Set ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á Selectors. CSS Selectors ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ HTML ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶è Style ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ Design ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ CSS ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ Selector ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡¶É
    
    - CSS Element Selector.
    - CSS Id Selector.
    - CSS Class Selector.
    - CSS Universal Selector.
    - CSS Group Selector.
    - CSS Attribute Selector
    
    ### CSS Element Selector:
    
    CSS Element Selector ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ HTML Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Name ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶á Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø **`<p>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Style ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá Element Name **`p`** ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá  Style ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡•§ Example: 
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          p{
              text-align: center;
              color: red;
            } 
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <p>Every paragraph will be affected by the style.</p>
        <p>Me too!</p>
        <p>And me!</p>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `p` ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá CSS Element Selector. ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ  Declaration ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Name ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá Style ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ 
    
    
   > üí° _Note_: CSS Element Selector ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶Æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® HTML Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Name ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Style ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ Website ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Same Element ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á Style ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Id ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Class Selector ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡•§

    
    ### CSS Id Selector:
    
    CSS Id Selector ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ HTML Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Id Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Specific Element ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá Style ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Id Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Unique Element Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Style ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Id Attribute ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Single Element ‡¶ï‡ßá Style ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ CSS Id Selector ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Web Page ‡¶è, Unique ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Page ‡¶è Same ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á Id ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ CSS Id Selector Use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Id Name ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá(#) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```css
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          #para1 {
            text-align: center;
            color: red;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <p id="para1">Hello World!</p>
        <p>This paragraph is not affected by the style.</p>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    - ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **`#para1`** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ CSS Id Selector ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ Declaration ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ (#) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Browser ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ú‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Id Selector  ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á Website HTML file ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá  **`#para1`** ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á Id Selector ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
    
    ### **CSS Class Selector:**
    
    CSS Class Selector ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ HTML Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Class Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï Element ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá Style ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Class Selector ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Element ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï Element ‡¶ï‡ßá Same Style ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ Code ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Website ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá CSS Class Selector ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ CSS Class Selector Use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Class Name ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá(.) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .center {
            text-align: center;
            color: red;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <h1 class="center">Red and center-aligned heading</h1>
        <p class="center">Red and center-aligned paragraph.</p>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    - ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **`.center`** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ CSS Class Selector ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ  Declaration ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ (.) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Browser ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ú‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Class Selector.
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á Class Selector ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ HTML Element ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Style ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá Element Name ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá Class Selector ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          p.center {
            text-align: center;
            color: red;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <h1 class="center">This heading will not be affected</h1>
        <p class="center">This paragraph will be red and center-aligned.</p>
      </body>
    </html> 
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ HTML Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ **`Class`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï Class ‡¶ï‡ßá Refer ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **`Class`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï Class ‡¶ï‡ßá reference ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§  Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
          <style>
            p.center {
                text-align: center;
                color: red;
              }
            p.large {
                font-size: 300%;
              }
          </style>
        </head>
        <body>
          <h1 class="center">This heading will not be affected</h1>
          <p class="center">This paragraph will be red and center-aligned.</p>
          <p class="center large">This paragraph will be red, center-aligned, and in a large font-size.</p> 
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### **CSS Universal Selector:**
    
    Universal Selector(*) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Elements ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá Style ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
          <style>
            *{
              text-align: center;
              color: blue;
            }
          </style>
        </head>
        <body>
          <h1>Hello world!</h1>
          <p>Every element on the page will be affected by the style.</p>
          <p id="para1">Me too!</p>
          <p>And me!</p>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### **CSS Group Selector:**
    
    CSS Group Selector ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Element ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá Same Style ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Code Minimize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ Group Selector ‡¶ï‡ßá Comma( , ) ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ 
    
    ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø **`<h1>`** Tag ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Design ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Same Design ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`<h2>`** Tag ‡¶ì **`<p>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ Same code ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```css
    h1 {
      text-align: center;
      color: red;
    }
    
    h2 {
      text-align: center;
      color: red;
    }
    
    p {
      text-align: center;
      color: red;
    }
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Same Declarations ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø Element Selector ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá  Group Selector ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Code ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Minimize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
          <style>
            h1, h2, p {
                  text-align: center;
                  color: red;
              }
          </style>
        </head>
        <body>
          <h1>Hello World!</h1>
          <h2>Smaller heading!</h2>
          <p>This is a paragraph.</p>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### CSS Attribute Selector:
    
    **CSS Attribute Selector** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø CSS ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ HTML Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ CSS Class ‡¶¨‡¶æ Id Selector ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ö‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ Attribute Selector ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Attribute ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ì‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Style ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    
    **CSS Attribute Selector ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶π:**
    
    - **[attribute]** ‚Üí ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Attribute ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
    - **[attribute="value"]** ‚Üí ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
    - **[attribute~="value"]** ‚Üí ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
    - **[attribute^="value"]** ‚Üí ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Word ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
    - **[attribute$="value"]** ‚Üí ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Word ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
    - **[attribute\*="value"]** ‚Üí ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü  ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
    - **[attribute|="value"]** ‚Üí ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Word ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
    
    1. **CSS `[attribute]` Selector:** 
    
        ‡¶è‡¶á Selector ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á, Value ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶π‡ßã‡¶ï ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶®‡•§  Example: 
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html lang="en">
          <head>
            <style>
              /* ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã <a> ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ href Attribute ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá */
              a[href] {
                color: green;
              }
            </style>
          </head>
          <body>
            <a href="https://www.example.com">Visit Example</a>
            <a>No Link</a>
          </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ **`<a>`** Tag ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ **`href`** Attribute ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø Green Color ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßÄ‡ßü **`<a>`** ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ó‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá **`href`** Attribute ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã Color ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
    
    2. **CSS `[attribute="value"]` Selector:**
    
        ‡¶è‡¶á Selector ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html lang="en">
          <head>
            <style>
              /* ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã <input> ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ type Attribute "text" ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá */
              input[type="text"] {
                background-color: lightblue;
              }
            </style>
          </head>
          <body>
            <input type="text" placeholder="Enter your name" />
            <input type="password" placeholder="Enter password" />
          </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ **`<input>`** ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ó‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø **`type="text"`** Attribute ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶≤ background ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßÄ‡ßü **`<input>`** ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßá **`type="password"`** Attribute ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

    3. **CSS `[attribute~="value"]` Selector:**
    
        ‡¶è‡¶á Selector ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Word ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **`~`** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Word ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶ñ‡ßã‡¶Å‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html lang="en">
          <head>
            <style>
              /* ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã <a> ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ class ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá "active" word ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá */
              a[class~="active"] {
                color: red;
              }
            </style>
          </head>
          <body>
            <a class="active nav-link">Home</a>
            <a class="nav-link">About</a>
            <a class="nav-link">Contact</a>
          </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ **`<a>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ **`class`** Attribute Value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **`"active"`**  word ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø Red Color ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßÄ‡ßü ‡¶ì ‡¶§‡ßÉ‡¶§‡ßÄ‡ßü  **`<a>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ **`class`** Attribute Value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **`"active"`** Word ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ Color ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

    4. **CSS `[attribute^="value"]` Selector:**
    
        ‡¶è‡¶á Selector ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Word  ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `^` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá Word ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶ñ‡ßã‡¶Å‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html lang="en">
          <head>
            <style>
              /* ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã <a> ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ href ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü "https://" ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡ßü */
              a[href^="https://"]
              {
                color: green;
              }
            </style>
          </head>
          <body>
            <a href="https://www.example.com">Example 1</a>
            <a href="http://www.test.com">Test 1</a>
          </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ **`<a>`** Tag ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ **`href`** Attribute Value  **`https://`** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø Green Color ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßÄ‡ßü **`<a>`** Tag ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ **`href`** Attribute Value  **`http://`** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

    5. **CSS `[attribute$="value"]` Selector:**
    
        ‡¶è‡¶á Selector ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Word  ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **`$`** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá Word ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶ñ‡ßã‡¶Å‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html lang="en">
          <head>
            <style>
              /* ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã <a> ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ href ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü ".com" ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡ßü */
              a[href$=".com"] {
                font-weight: bold;
              }
            </style>
          </head>
          <body>
            <a href="https://www.example.com">Example Link</a>
            <a href="https://www.test.org">Test Link</a>
          </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ **`<a>`** Tag ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ **`href`** Attribute Value **`.com`** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø Bold ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßÄ‡ßü **`<a>`** Tag ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ **`href`** Attribute Value **`.org`** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø Bold ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

    6. **CSS `[attribute*="value"]` Selector:**
    
        ‡¶è‡¶á Selector ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Word  ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **`*`** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Word ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶ñ‡ßã‡¶Å‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html lang="en">
          <head>
            <style>
              /* ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã <a> ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ href ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü‡ßá "example" ‡¶∂‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶¶ ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá */
              a[href*="example"] {
                color: green;
              }
            </style>
          </head>
          <body>
            <a href="https://www.example.com">Example Link</a>
            <a href="https://www.testexample.com">Test Example Link</a>
            <a href="https://www.othertest.com">Other Test Link</a>
          </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø **`<a>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ **`href`** Attribute Value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **`"example"`** ‡¶∂‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ Green Color ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡ßÉ‡¶§‡ßÄ‡ßü **`<a>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ **`href`** Attribute Value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **`"example"`** ‡¶∂‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

    6. **CSS `[attribute|="value"]` Selector:**

        ‡¶è‡¶á Selector ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® Element Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Word ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶´‡ßá‡¶® `-`) ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° (language code) ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ó‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html lang="en">
          <head>
            <style>
              /* ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ lang ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü "en" ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ "en-" ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡ßü */
              p[lang|="en"] {
                font-family: Arial, sans-serif;
                color: blue;
              }
            </style>
          </head>
          <body>
            <p lang="en">English Heading</p>
            <p lang="en-US">This is English (United States)</p>
            <p lang="en-GB">This is English (Great Britain)</p>
            <p lang="fr">Ceci est un texte en fran√ßais.</p>
          </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ, ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßÄ‡ßü, ‡¶§‡ßÉ‡¶§‡ßÄ‡ßü **`p`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ **`lang`** Attribute value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **`en`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`en-`** ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ font ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç color ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡ß™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• **`p`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ **`lang`** Attribute value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **`fr`** ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶∞ font ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç color ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
        
        ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ç CSS Attribute Selectors ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Tool ‡¶Ø‡¶æ HTML Element ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ Attribute  ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç  Value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Styling ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Selector ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Element ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Customize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶¨‡¶æ Value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
    
        ---
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá HTML Documents ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá CSS ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü?
    
    HTML Document ‡¶ï‡ßá Style ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á CSS ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá CSS ‡¶ï‡ßá HTML Document ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ 
    
    - Inline CSS
    - Internal CSS
    - External CSS.
    
    ### **Inline CSS:**
    
    Inline CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ HTML ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡•§ Inline CSS ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶á **`style`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá CSS Syntax ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Single Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Unique Style ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <body>
            <h1 style="color:blue;text-align:center;">This is a heading</h1>
            <p style="color:red;">This is a paragraph.</p>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ### **Internal CSS:**
    
    Internal CSS ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Single Document ‡¶¨‡¶æ Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ Style ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ Internal CSS ‡¶è‡¶á Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Elements ‡¶ï‡ßá Style ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Internal CSS ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü HTML Document ‡¶è‡¶∞ **`<head>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá **`<style>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
          <style>
            body {
                background-color: linen;
              }
            h1 {
                color: maroon;
                text-align:center;
              } 
          </style>
        </head>
        <body>
          <h1>This is a heading</h1>
          <p>This is a paragraph.</p>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ### External CSS:
    
    External CSS ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Multiple Pages ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Page ‡¶ï‡ßá Style ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ External CSS ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø File ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ HTML File ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá Extension ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨ **`.css`** ‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® File Path ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá **`style.css`** ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **style** ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá File Name ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`.css`**  ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá File Extension. File Name ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ File Extension ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á **`.css`** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ File ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á File ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ CSS Style ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example:
    
    ```css
    body {
      background-color: lightblue;
    }
    
    h1 {
      color: navy;
      text-align:center;
    }
    ```
    
    Inline ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Internal CSS ‡¶è **`<style>`** Tag ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶á File ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø HTML Document ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á File ‡¶ü‡¶ø HTML File ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá Link ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Link ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`<link>`** Tag ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ CSS File ‡¶ü‡¶ø Link ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø **`<head>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **`<link>`** Tag ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
          <link rel="stylesheet" href="style.css">
        </head>
        <body>
          <h1>This is a heading</h1>
          <p>This is a paragraph.</p>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    Link Complete ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá **`<link>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **`rel`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á File ‡¶ü‡¶ø Link ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ File(‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ stylesheet File.) ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`href`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá File path ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
    

    > üí° **_Note_:** Inline CSS ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Style ‡¶è‡¶á Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ Apply ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ CSS Rules ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á  Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá Style ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡ßü Browser Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`<h1>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø External CSS File(**style.css**) ‡¶è Style ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶Æ `color: red;` ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ Internal CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **`<h1>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Style ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶Æ `color: blue;` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç  **`<h1>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Inline CSS ‡¶è Style ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶Æ `color: green;` ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Browser ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Color ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá inline CSS ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé **`<h1>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ Color **green** ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶® Browser Always ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶∞ CSS ‡¶ü‡¶æ Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Inline CSS ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá? ‡¶â‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Internal CSS ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé **`<h1>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ Color **blue** ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ Internal CSS ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ Code ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Override ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü‡¶ï‡¶•‡¶æ Highest Priority ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Inline CSS. ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Inline CSS ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
   
    ---
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Comment ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá?
    
    HTML Comments ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ CSS Comments ‡¶ì Browser ‡¶è Display ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé Browser ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Ignore ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ HTML ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Code ‡¶è‡¶∞ Explanation ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ CSS Comment ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Comment ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡ßá Developer ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® Code ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßú‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ Code ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ CSS Comment ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü **`/* ‚Ä¶‚Ä¶.. */`**  ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>  
    <html>  
        <head>  
          <style>  
              p {  
                  color: blue;   /* This is a single-line comment */  
                  text-align: center; /* This is a single-line comment */ 
                }   
              /* This is  
                  a multi-line  
                  comment */  
          </style>  
        </head>  
        <body>  
          <p>Hello</p>  
          <p>This statement is styled with CSS.</p>  
          <p>CSS comments are ignored by the browsers and not shown in the output.</p>  
        </body>  
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á CSS Colors ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
    
    CSS ‡¶è Color Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Color Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Font Color ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Background Color Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® CSS Border Color ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ 
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶®‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Color ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø:
    
    - RGB format.
    - RGBA format.
    - Hexadecimal notation.
    - HSL.
    - HSLA.
    - Built-in color.
    
    ### RGB Format:
    
    RGB ‡¶´‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶≤ 'RED, GREEN ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç BLUE'-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ 0 ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 255-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá R, G, B-‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø HTML Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Color Define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Format Use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø **`rgb()`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Property ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ Values ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Property Value Percentage ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ Integer(0 ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 255) ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Example: 
    
    RGB Syntax: **`rgb(red, green, blue)`**  
    
    - Black Color: **`rgb(0,0,0)`**
    - White Color: **`rgb(255,255,255)`**
    - Red Color: **`rgb(255, 0 , 0)`**
    
    ‡¶è‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Value Change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® Color ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§
    
    ---
    
    ### RGBA Format:
    
    RGBA Format ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ RGB Format ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ Extra ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Alpha Value Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Color Transparency ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ Alpha Value Range 0.0 ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 1 ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Alpha Value 0.0 ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Element Color ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ Transparent ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ Alpha Value 1 ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Transparent ‡¶®‡ßü‡•§ Example:
    
    **RGBA Syntax:** **`rgba(red,green,blue,alpha)`**   **`rgba(255,99,71,0.6)`**
    
    ---
    
    ### Hexadecimal Notation:
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Hexadecimal Value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶ì CSS Color ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Hexadecimal Notation ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡ßü (#) Symbol ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá Six Digit ‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Color Representation ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Six Digit Characters ‡¶è‡¶∞ Range  ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá 0 ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá F ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ Digit Represent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Red(RR) Color Value ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ Digits Represent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Green(GG) Color Value ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ Digit Represent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Blue(BB) Color Value ‡¶ï‡ßá. Example:
    
    HEX Value Syntax: **`#(0-F)(0-F)(0-F)(0-F)(0-F)(0-F)`**
    
    - Black Color: **`#000000`**
    - White Color: **`#ffffff`**
    - Red Color: **`#ff0000`**
    
    ‡¶è‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Value Change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® Color ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá 3 Digit ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶ì HEX Color ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Short HEX Value ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Example:
    
    - Black Color: **`#000`**
    - White Color: **`#fff`**
    - Red Color: **`#f00`**
    
    ---
    
    ### HSL Value:
    
    HSL ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Hue, Saturation ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Lightness ‡¶è‡¶∞ Short form. 
    
    **Hue:**  ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶≤ 0 ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 360 ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ Color Wheel ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá 0 ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Red Color, 120 ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Green Color ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç 240 ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Blue Color. 
    
    **Saturation:** ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Percentage Value. ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá 0% ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Shade of Gray Color ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç 100% ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ Color.
    
    **Lightness**: ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ì Saturation ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ Percentage Value ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ 0% ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü Black, 50% ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü Not Light, Not Dark ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç 100% ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ White Color.
    
    Example: 
    
    HSL Value Syntax: **`hsl(*hue*,¬†*saturation*,¬†*lightness*)`**
    
    - Red Color: **`hsl(0,100%,50%)`**
    - Blue Color: **`hsl(240,100%,50%)`**
    - Green Color: **`hsl(150,50%,50%)`**
    
    ---
    
    ### HSLA Value:
    
    HLSA Value ‡¶ì HSL Value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá RGBA Value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ Alpha Value Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Color Transparency ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ Alpha Value Range 0.0 ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 1 ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Alpha Value 0.0 ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Element Color ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ Transparent ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ Alpha Value 1 ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Transparent ‡¶®‡ßü‡•§ Example: 
    
    HSLA Value Syntax: **`hsla(*hue,*¬†*saturation*,¬†*lightness, alpha*)`  `hsla(9, 100%, 64%, 0.8)`**
    
    ---
    
    ### **Build-in Color:**
    
    Build-in Color ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Color ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Red, Green, Blue, Orange ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    Build-in Color Syntax: **`color: color-name;`**  **`color: red;`**  
    
    ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Build-in Color ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á Color ‡¶è‡¶∞ HEX Value ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç RGB Value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Table ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤:
    
    | S.no. | Color name | Hexadecimal Value |     RGB value |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | **1.** | Red | #FF0000 | rgb(255,0,0) |
    | **2.** | Orange | #FFA500 | rgb(255,165,0) |
    | **3.** | Yellow | #FFFF00 | rgb(255,255,0) |
    | **4.** | Pink | #FFC0CB | rgb(255,192,203) |
    | **5.** | Green | #008000 | rgb(0,128,0) |
    | **6.** | Violet | #EE82EE | rgb(238,130,238) |
    | **7.** | Blue | #0000FF | rgb(0,0,255) |
    | **8.** | Aqua | #00FFFF | rgb(0,255,255) |
    | **9.** | Brown | #A52A2A | rgb(165,42,42) |
    | **10.** | White | #FFFFFF | rgb(255,255,255) |
    | **11.** | Gray | #808080 | rgb(128,128,128) |
    | **12.** | Black | #000000 | rgb(0,0,0) |
    
    > ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Browser Support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡ßß‡ß™‡ß¶‡¶ü‡¶ø Colors Name and HEX Value Link ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡•§
    
    
    [HTML Color Names](https://www.w3schools.com/colors/colors_names.asp)
    
    
    > üí° **_Note_:** RGB Value ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Browser Support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶ß ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Browser Support ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ Plan ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
    
    ---
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á CSS Background Property ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
    
    CSS Background Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Background Effects ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ CSS ‡¶è ‡ß´ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ Background Properties ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Background Effects ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡¶É
    
    - background-color
    - background-image
    - background-repeat
    - background-position
    - background-attachment
    - background-size
    
    ### CSS background-color:
    
    CSS **`background-color`**  Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Background Color ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
          <style>
            body {
                background-color: lightblue;
            }
          </style>
        </head>
        <body>
          <h1>Hello World!</h1>
          <p>This page has a light blue background color!</p>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá CSS Color ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Color ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® HEX Color, HSL Color ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§
    
    ---
    
    ### CSS background-image:
    
    CSS **`background-image`** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Background Image Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ By Default Image Repeated ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ Element ‡¶ï‡ßá Cover ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Image ‡¶è‡¶∞ Size Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Size Ratio ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Background ‡¶è Image Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá CSS Property Value ‡¶§‡ßá **`url(‚Äùimage path‚Äù)`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
          <style>
            body {
                background-image: url("paper.gif");
              }
          </style>
        </head>
        <body>
          <h1>Hello World!</h1>
          <p>This page has an image as the background!</p>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    Background Image ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ö‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá Text Color ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ Background Image Color ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡ßá Website ‡¶è‡¶∞  Text ‡¶™‡ßú‡¶§‡ßá User ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
          <style>
            body {
                background-image: url("bgdesert.jpg");
              }
          </style>
        </head>
        <body>
          <h1>Hello World!</h1>
          <p>This text is not easy to read on this background image.</p>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ Text ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Background Image ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Bad Combination. ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Text ‡¶™‡ßú‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® Background Image Use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ Text ‡¶™‡ßú‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Disturb ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
    
    ---
    
    ### CSS background-repeat:
    
    By Default, Background Image Size ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Size Ratio ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® **`background-image`** Property Image ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Repeats ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Horizontally(‡¶Ü‡ßú‡¶æ-‡¶Ü‡ßú‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá) ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Vertically(‡¶≤‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ-‡¶≤‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá). ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Image ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Repeat ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ Horizontally Or Vertically. ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ù‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
          <style>
            body {
                background-image: url("gradient_bg.png");
              }
          </style>
        </head>
        <body>
          <h1>Hello World!</h1>
          <p>Strange background image...</p>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ Image ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ Horizontally Repeat ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá (**`background-repeat: repeat-x;`**) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá Background Image ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
          <style>
            body {
                background-image: url("gradient_bg.png");
                background-repeat: repeat-x;
              }
          </style>
        </head>
        <body>
          <h1>Hello World!</h1>
          <p>Here, a background image is repeated only horizontally!</p>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    
    >üí° **_Note_:** ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Background Image ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Vertically Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá (**`background-repeat: repeat-y;`**) Use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
    
    ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø **`background-image`** ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ Repeating ‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá (**`background-repeat: no-repeat;`**) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
            <style>
                    body {
                      background-image: url("img_tree.png");
                      background-repeat: no-repeat;
                    }
            </style>
        </head>
        <body>
                <h1>Hello World!</h1>
                <p>W3Schools background image example.</p>
                <p>The background image only shows once, but it is disturbing the reader!</p>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ### **CSS background-position:**
    
    CSS **`background-position`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Background Image ‡¶è‡¶∞ Initial Position(‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶õ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá) Define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ By Default Webpage ‡¶è Background Image Top-Left(‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá) ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã Value ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Background Position Value ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    
    - center
    - top
    - bottom
    - left
    - right
    
    Example:
    
    ```html

                <p>This is a fixed background-image. Scroll down the page.</p>
                <p>This is a fixed background-image. Scroll down the page.</p>
                <p>This is a fixed background-image. Scroll down the page.</p>
                <p>This is a fixed background-image. Scroll down the page.</p>
                <p>This is a fixed background-image. Scroll down the page.</p>
                <p>This is a fixed background-image. Scroll down the page.</p>
    ```

    ### CSS background-attachment:
    
    CSS **`background-attachment`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Web Page Scroll ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü Background Image Scroll ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø Fixed ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ Background Image Fixed ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá (**`background-attachment: fixed;`**) ‡¶è‡¶á Property Value ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
