    ### **CSS background - Shorthand property:**
    
    CSS Background ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® CSS background Property ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï Line ‡¶è ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Shorthand Property. Shorthand Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Code ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡ßá, CSS Code ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ CSS ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶Æ Shorthand Property ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ Shorthand Property Syntax: **`background: background-color background-image background-repeat background-attachment background-position`**   Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
                <style>
                        body {
                      background: #ffffff url("img_tree.png") no-repeat fixed right top;
                      margin-right: 200px;
                    }
                </style>
        </head>
        <body>
                <h1>The background Property</h1>
                <p>The background property is a shorthand property for specifying all the background properties in one declaration.</p>
                <p>Here, the background image is only shown once, and it is also positioned in the top-right corner.</p>
                <p>We have also added a right margin, so that the text will not write over the background image.</p>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Property ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶•‡¶æ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
            <style>
                    body {
                      background: skyblue;
                }
            </style>
        </head>
        <body>
                <h1>The background Property</h1>
                <p>The background property is a shorthand property for specifying all the background properties in one declaration.</p>
                <p>Here, the background image is only shown once, and it is also positioned in the top-right corner.</p>
                <p>We have also added a right margin, so that the text will not write over the background image.</p>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ### CSS Background-size:
    
    CSS **`background-size`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Background Image ‡¶è‡¶∞ Size Define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
            <style>
                #example2 {
                      border: 2px solid black;
                      padding: 25px;
                      background: url(mountain.jpg);
                      background-repeat: no-repeat;
                      background-size: 300px 100px;
                    }
                #example1 {
                      border: 2px solid black;
                      padding: 25px;
                      background: url(mountain.jpg);
                      background-repeat: no-repeat;
                      background-size: auto;
                    }
                #example3 {
                      border: 2px solid black;
                      padding: 25px;
                      background: url(mountain.jpg);
                      background-repeat: no-repeat;
                      background-size: cover;
                    }
                #example4 {
                      border: 2px solid black;
                      padding: 25px;
                      background: url(mountain.jpg);
                        background-repeat: no-repeat;
                      background-size: contain;
                    }
                #example5 {
                      border: 2px solid black;
                      padding: 25px;
                      background: url(mountain.jpg);
                      background-repeat: no-repeat;
                      background-size: 50%;
                    }
            </style>
        </head>
        <body>
          <h2>background-size: 300px 100px:</h2>
                <div id="example2">
                      <h2>Hello World</h2>
                      <p>Here, the background image is set to 300px wide and 100px high.</p>
                </div>
    
                <h2>background-size: auto (default):</h2>
                <div id="example1">
                      <h2>Hello World</h2>
                      <p>The background image is displayed in its original size.</p>
                </div>
    
                <h2>background-size: cover</h2>
                <div id="example3">
                      <h2>Hello World</h2>
                      <p>The background image is displayed in its cover size.</p>
                </div>
    
                <h2>background-size: contain</h2>
                <div id="example4">
                      <h2>Hello World</h2>
                      <p>The background image is displayed in its contain size.</p>
                </div>
    
                <h2>background-size: percentage</h2>
                <div id="example5">
                      <h2>Hello World</h2>
                      <p>The background image is displayed in its contain size.</p>
                </div>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£  ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ Box Model ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
    
    ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø HTML Elements ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Box ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ CSS ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® Design ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Layout ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶•‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‚Äúbox-model‚Äù ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶•‡¶æ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Box-Model ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Box ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø HTML Elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡ßú‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü margin, border, padding and actual Content of Element ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá Box-Model ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶õ‡¶¨‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡¶É
    
    ![CSS Box Model.png](CSS_Box_Model.png)
    
    ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡ß™‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶É
    
    - Content ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Content ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá Box ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ Text ‡¶¨‡¶æ Image ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
    - Padding ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Padding ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡ßü Content ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Border ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Padding ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Transparent ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé Padding ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Color ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
    - Border ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Border ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü Content ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Padding ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∞ area ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
    - Margin ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Margin ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü Border ‡¶è‡¶∞ Outside Area ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Margin ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Transparent ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé Margin ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Color ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
    
    Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
            <style>
              *{
                            box-sizing: border-box;
                 }
                    .other-box1{
                        border: 5px solid black;
                    }
                    .box1 {
                          background-color: lightgrey;
                          border: 5px solid green;
                          padding: 30px;
                          margin: 20px;
                    }
                .other-box2{
                     border: 5px solid black;
                    }
                .box2 {
                       background-color: lightgrey;
                       border: 5px solid green;
                       padding: 30px;
                    }
                .other-box3{
                     border: 5px solid black;
                    }
                .box3 {
                          background-color: lightgrey;
                          border: 5px solid green;
                          margin: 30px;
                    }
            </style>
        </head>
        <body>
                <h2>Demonstrating the Box Model</h2>
                <h3> With Margin, Border,Padding </h3>
                <div class="other-box1">
                        <div class="box1"> This is My Content</div>
                </div>
    
                <h3>With Border and Padding But Without Margin </h3>
                <div class="other-box2">
                        <div class="box2"> This is My Content</div>
                </div>
    
                <h3>With Border and Margin But Without Padding </h3>
                <div class="other-box3">
                        <div class="box3"> This is My Content</div>
                </div>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    - ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® CSS Padding Properties ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á‡•§
        
        ### CSS Padding:
        
        CSS **`padding`** Properties ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Border ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Content ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡ßá Space ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ Padding ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Transparent ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∞ Setting Control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Padding ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü Top, Right, Bottom ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Left Side ‡¶è‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Individual ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ 
        
        - **padding-top** : ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá Padding ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§
        - **padding-right**: ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Padding ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§
        - **padding-bottom** : ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá Padding ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§
        - **padding-left**: ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá Padding ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§
        
        ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Padding Properties ‡¶è‡¶∞ Values ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
        
        - **length ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá**: Length ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Padding Value `px`, `pt`, `cm` ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§
        - **percentage ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá**: Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá % ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á Value ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
        
        Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
            <head>
                    <style>
                            div {
                                  border: 1px solid black;
                                  background-color: lightblue;
                                  padding-top: 50px;
                                  padding-right: 30px;
                                  padding-bottom: 50px;
                                  padding-left: 80px;
                            }
                </style>
            </head>
            <body>
                    <h2>Using individual padding properties</h2>
                    <div>This div element has a top padding of 50px, a right padding of 30px, a bottom padding of 50px, and a left padding of 80px.</div>
            </body>
        </html>
        ```
        > üí° Note: Negative Value ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Allow ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
        
        ### Padding Shorthand Property:
        
        Background Shorthand Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ Padding ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ì Shorthand Property ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Padding Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡ß™‡¶ü‡¶ø Value ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§
        
        **Padding 4 Value  Shorthand Syntax**:  **`padding: top right bottom left`  `padding: 25px 50px 75px 100px;`**
        
        **Padding 3 Value  Shorthand Syntax:**  **`padding: top (right and left) bottom`   `padding: 25px 50px 75px;`**
        
        **Padding 2 Value  Shorthand Syntax:**  **`padding: (top and  bottom) (right and left)`  `padding: 25px 50px;`**
        
        **Padding 1 Value  Shorthand Syntax:**  **`padding: (All Sides)`  `padding: 25px;`**

        ---

    - ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® CSS Border Properties ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á‡•§
        
        ### CSS Border:
        
        CSS **`border`** Properties ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Border ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Border ‡¶è‡¶∞ Style, Color ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Size ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ CSS **`border`** Properties ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡¶É
        
        - border-style
        - border-color
        - border-width
        - border-radius
        
        ### CSS Border Style:
        
        CSS **`border-style`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Web Page ‡¶è Border ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞  Type ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá **`border-style`** Values ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡¶É
        
        | Value | Description |
        | --- | --- |
        | none | ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® border ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§  |
        | dotted | ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ dotted border ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ |
        | dashed | ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ dashed border ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ |
        | solid | ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ solid border ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ |
        | double | ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá double border ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ |
        | groove | ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ 3d grooved border ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá effect ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü border-color value ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ |
        | ridge | ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ 3d ridged border ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá effect ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü border-color value ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ |
        | inset | ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ 3d inset border ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá effect ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü border-color value ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ |
        | outset | ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ 3d outset border ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá effect ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü border-color value ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ |
        
        Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
            <head>
              <style>
                p.dotted {border-style: dotted;}
                p.dashed {border-style: dashed;}
                p.solid {border-style: solid;}
                p.double {border-style: double;}
                p.groove {border-style: groove;}
                p.ridge {border-style: ridge;}
                p.inset {border-style: inset;}
                p.outset {border-style: outset;}
                p.none {border-style: none;}
                p.hidden {border-style: hidden;}
              </style>
            </head>
            <body>
              <h2>The border-style Property</h2>
              <p>‡¶è‡¶á Property ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ Border Display ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá:</p>
        
              <p class="dotted">A dotted border.</p>
              <p class="dashed">A dashed border.</p>
              <p class="solid">A solid border.</p>
              <p class="double">A double border.</p>
              <p class="groove">A groove border.</p>
              <p class="ridge">A ridge border.</p>
              <p class="inset">An inset border.</p>
              <p class="outset">An outset border.</p>
              <p class="none">No border.</p>
              <p class="hidden">A hidden border.</p>	
            </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Mix Border Style ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé Top, Right, Bottom, Left Side ‡¶è Individual ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ Style ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
            <head>
              <style>
                .mix {
                      border-style: dotted dashed solid double;
                    }
              </style>
            </head>
            <body>
              <h2>The border-style Property</h2>
              <p class="mix">A mixed border.</p>
            </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        **Mix 4 value Border Style Syntax**: **`border-style: top-border right-border bottom-border left-border`** Example: **`border-style: dotted solid double dashed;`**
        
        **Mix 3 value Border Style Syntax**: **`border-style: top-border (right-border and left-border) bottom-border`**  Example: **`border-style: dotted solid double;`**
        
        **Mix 2 value Border Style Syntax**: **`border-style: (top-border and bottom-border) (right-border and left-border)`** Example:  **`border-style: solid double;`**
        
        ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá  **`border-top-style`**, **`border-right-style`**, **`border-bottom-style`** ,**`border-left-style`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Border ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø Side ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Style ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
            <head>
              <style>
                p {
                  border-top-style: dashed;
                  border-right-style: solid;
                  border-bottom-style: dotted;
                  border-left-style: double;
                }
              </style>
            </head>
            <body>
              <h2>Individual Border Side Style</h2>
              <p>4 different border styles.</p>
            </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ---
        
        ### CSS border-color:
        
        CSS **`border-color`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Border ‡¶è‡¶∞ Color ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ CSS Color ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Color ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Solid Color(color name), `**hex`, `hsl`** ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
            <head>
              <style>
                p.one {
                  border-style: solid;
                  border-color: red;
                }
                
                p.two {
                  border-style: solid;
                  border-color: green;
                } 
      
                p.three {
                  border-style: dotted;
                  border-color: blue;
                } 
              </style>
            </head>
            <body>
              <h2>The border-color Property</h2>
              <p>This property specifies the color of the four borders:</p>
              
              <p class="one">A solid red border</p>
              <p class="two">A solid green border</p>
              <p class="three">A dotted blue border</p>
              
              <p><b>Note:</b> The "border-color" property ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ "border-style" Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü Color ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá "border-style" Property ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ </p>
            </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Mix Border Color ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§  ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé Top, Right, Bottom, Left Side ‡¶è Individual ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ Color ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
            <head>
              <style>
                p.one {
                  border-style: solid;
                  border-color: red green blue yellow; /* red top, green right, blue bottom and yellow left */
                }
              </style>
            </head>
            <body>
              <h2>The border-color Property</h2>
              <p>The border-color property can have from one to four values (for the top border, right border, bottom border, and the left border):</p>
              <p class="one">A solid multicolor border</p>
            </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`border-top-color`**,**`border-right-color`**,**`border-bottom-color`** ,**`border-left-color`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Border ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø Side ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Color ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
            <head>
              <style>
                p {
                  border-style: dashed;
                  border-top-color: orange;
                  border-right-color: red;
                  border-bottom-color: blue;
                  border-left-color: green;
                }
              </style>
            </head>
            <body>
              <h2>Individual Border Side Color</h2>
              <p>4 different border Color.</p>
            </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ---
        
        ### CSS border-width:
        
        CSS **`border-width`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Border ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Width ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`in`**, **`px`**, **`cm`**, **`em`** ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Width Size ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ Pre-Define Value ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶ì Size ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤ **thin**, **medium**, **thick**. Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
            <head>
                <style>
                  p.one {
                    border-style: solid;
                    border-width: 5px;
                  }
                  
                  p.two {
                    border-style: solid;
                    border-width: medium;
                  }
                  
                  p.three {
                    border-style: dotted;
                    border-width: 2px;
                  }
                  
                  p.four {
                    border-style: dotted;
                    border-width: thick;
                  }
                  
                  p.five {
                    border-style: double;
                    border-width: 15px;
                  }
                  
                  p.six {
                    border-style: double;
                    border-width: thick;
                  }
                </style>
            </head>
            <body>
              <h2>The border-width Property</h2>
              <p>This property specifies the width of the four borders:</p>
              
              <p class="one">5px border-width</p>
              <p class="two">medium border-width</p>
              <p class="three">2px border-width</p>
              <p class="four">thick border-width</p>
              <p class="five">15px border-width</p>
              <p class="six">thick border-width</p>
              
              <p><b>Note:</b> "border-width" Property ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ "border-style" Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü Width ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá "border-style" Property ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ </p>
            </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Mix Border Width ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§  ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé Top, Right, Bottom, Left Side ‡¶è Individual ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ Width ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
            <head>
                <style>
                  p.one {
                    border-style: solid;
                    border-width: 5px 20px; /* 5px top and bottom, 20px on the sides */
                  }
                  
                  p.two {
                    border-style: solid;
                    border-width: 20px 5px; /* 20px top and bottom, 5px on the sides */
                  }
                  
                  p.three {
                    border-style: solid;
                    border-width: 25px 10px 4px 35px; /* 25px top, 10px right, 4px bottom and 35px left */
                  }
                </style>
            </head>
            <body>
              <h2>The border-width Property</h2>
              <p>The border-width property can have from one to four values (for the top border, right border, bottom border, and the left border):</p>
          
              <p class="one">Some text.</p>
              <p class="two">Some text.</p>
              <p class="three">Some text.</p>
            </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`border-top-width`**,**`border-right-width`**,**`border-bottom-width`**,**`border-left-width`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Border ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø Side ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Width ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
            <head>
              <style>
                p {
                  border-style: dashed;
                  border-top-width: 5px;
                  border-right-width: 10px;
                  border-bottom-width: 15px;
                  border-left-width: 20px;
                }
              </style>
            </head>
            <body>
              <h2>Individual Border Side Width</h2>
              <p>4 different border width.</p>
            </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        **CSS Border Shorthand Property:**
        
        ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá CSS Border Shorthand Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ Properties ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï Line ‡¶è ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
        
        **CSS Border Shorthand Property Syntax**: **`border: border-width border-style(‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá) border-color`** Example: **`border: 5px solid red;`  `border: 10px dashed blue;`**
        
        ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`border-top`**, **`border-right`**, **`border-bottom`**, **`border-left`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Individual Style ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
            <head>
              <style>
                .left {
                  border-left: 6px solid red;
                  background: skyblue;
                }
                .top {
                  border-top: 6px solid red;
                  background: skyblue;
                }
                .right {
                  border-right: 6px solid red;
                  background: skyblue;
                }
                .bottom {
                  border-bottom: 6px solid red;
                  background: skyblue;
                }
              </style>
            </head>
            <body>
              <h2>The border-left Property</h2>
              <p class="left">This property is a shorthand property for border-left-width, border-left-style, and border-left-color.</p>
              
              <h2>The border-top Property</h2>
              <p class="top">This property is a shorthand property for border-top-width, border-top-style, and border-top-color.</p>
              
              <h2>The border-right Property</h2>
              <p class="right">This property is a shorthand property for border-right-width, border-right-style, and border-right-color.</p>
              
              <h2>The border-bottom Property</h2>
              <p class="bottom">This property is a shorthand property for border-bottom-width, border-bottom-style, and border-bottom-color.</p>
            </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ---
        
        ### CSS Border Radius:
        
        CSS **`border-radius`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Border ‡¶è‡¶∞ Corner Side ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Round ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
            <head>
              <style>
                p.normal {
                  border: 2px solid red;
                  padding: 5px;
                }
                
                p.round1 {
                  border: 2px solid red;
                  border-radius:8px;
                  padding: 5px;
                }
                
                p.round2 {
                  border: 2px solid red;
                  border-radius: 10px;
                  padding: 5px;
                }
                
                p.round3 {
                  border: 2px solid red;
                  border-radius: 15px;
                  padding: 5px;
                }
              </style>
            </head>
            <body>
              <h2>The border-radius Property</h2>
              <p>This property is used to add rounded borders to an element:</p>
              
              <p class="normal">Normal border</p>
              <p class="round1">Round border 5px</p>
              <p class="round2">Rounder border 10px</p>
              <p class="round3">Roundest border 15px</p>
            </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Shorthand Property ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá Border ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡ß™‡¶ü‡¶ø Corner ‡¶ï‡ßá Control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
            <head>
            <style>
              .four{
                border: 2px solid red;
                border-radius: 5px 8px 12px 15px;
                padding: 5px;
              }
              .three{
                border: 2px solid red;
                border-radius: 5px 10px 15px;
                padding: 5px;
              }
              .two{
                border: 2px solid red;
                border-radius: 5px 10px;
                padding: 5px;
              }
            </style>
            </head>
            <body>
              <h2>The border-radius Property</h2>
              <p>This property is used to add rounded borders to an element:</p>
              
              <p class="four">Normal Text</p>
              <p class="three">Normal Text</p>
              <p class="two">Normal Text</p>
            </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ---
        
    - ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® CSS Margin Properties ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á‡•§
        
        ### CSS Margin:
        
        CSS **`margin`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü border ‡¶è‡¶∞ outside ‡¶è space ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ CSS Margin, Padding ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ transparent ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ setting ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ each Side control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ CSS **`margin`** Properties ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡¶É 
        
        - margin-top ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ Side ‡¶è Margin ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
        - margin-right ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ Side ‡¶è Margin ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
        - margin-bottom ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ Side ‡¶è Margin ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
        - margin-left ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∞ Side ‡¶è Margin ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
        
        ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`margin`** Properties ‡¶è‡¶∞ Values ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
        
        - **auto** ‚Üí Browser ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á Margin Calculate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
        - **length ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá**: Length ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Margin Value `px`, `pt`, `cm` ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§
        - **percentage ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá**: Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá % ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á Value ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
        - **inherit** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ height/width ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Parent Value ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
        
        Example: 
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
          <head>
            <style>
              div {
                background-color: lightblue;
                border: 1px solid black;
                margin-top: 100px;
                margin-bottom: 100px;
                margin-right: 150px;
                margin-left: 80px;
              }
            </style>
          </head>
          <body>
            <h2> Using individual margin properties </h2>
            <div> This div element has a top margin of 100px, a right margin of 150px, a bottom margin of 100px, and a left margin of 80px.
            </div>
          </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        > üí° Note: Negative Value ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Allow ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
        
        **CSS Margin Shorthand Property:**
        
        ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Shorthand Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Property ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ 
        
        **Margin 4 value Shorthand Property Syntax** : **`margin: top right bottom left`** Example:  **`margin: 25px 50px 75px 100px`**
        
        **Margin 3 value Shorthand Property Syntax** : **`margin: top right and left bottom`** Example:  **`margin: 25px 50px 75px`**
        
        **Margin 2 value Shorthand Property Syntax** : **`margin: (top and bottom) (right and left)**` Example:  **`margin: 25px 50px`**
        
        **Margin 1 value Shorthand Property Syntax**: **`margin: (All Sides)**` Example:  **`margin: 25px`**
        
        ### **The auto Value:**
        
        ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ Parent Container ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Horizontally Center ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶®‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Margin **`auto`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Width ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø Block Element ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Margin auto Property ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤ Parent Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶ø Space ‡¶ü‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßÅ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá Left ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Right Side Margin ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø Center ‡¶è ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
            <head>
            <style>
              div {
                width: 300px;
                margin: auto;
                border: 1px solid red;
              }
            </style>
            </head>
            <body>
            <h2>Use of margin: auto</h2>
            <div>
                This div will be horizontally centered because it has margin: auto;
            </div>
            </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ---
        
        ### The inherit Value:
        
        CSS **`margin`** Property Value **`inherit`** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Parent Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Margin Inherit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `<p class =‚Äùex1‚Äù>` Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Left Margin ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ Parent Element `<div>` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Inherited ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
            <head>
            <style>
              div {
                border: 1px solid red;
                margin-left: 100px;
              }
              
              p.ex1 {
                margin-left: inherit;
              }
            </style>
            </head>
            <body>
            <h2>Use of the inherit value</h2>
            <p>Let the left margin be inherited from the parent element:</p>
            
            <div>
            <p class="ex1">This paragraph has an inherited left margin (from the div element).</p>
            </div>
            </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ---
        
    - ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® CSS Height, Width and Max-width Properties ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á‡•§
        
        CSS **`height`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`width`** Properties ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Height ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Width Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ **`height`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`width`** Properties Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ Padding, Margin Border ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ Padding, Border ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Margin ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá Area ‡¶è‡¶∞ Height/Width Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
        
        CSS **`height`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`width`** Properties ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø Value Support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤:
        
        - **auto** - ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ Default ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Browser ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá Device ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá Height ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Width Value Calculate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
        - **length** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Height/Width ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value **`px`**, **`cm`**, **`in`** ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
        - **percentage(%)** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Element Container Block ‡¶è‡¶∞ Percentage ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Height/Width ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
        - **initial** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá height/width ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Default Value.
        - **inherit** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá height/width ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Parent ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
        
        Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
        <head>
            <style>
                *{
                    margin: 0;
                    padding: 0;
                    box-sizing: border-box;
                }
                .parent-div{
                    height: 100px;
                    width: 100%;
                    border: 2px solid blue;
                }
                .child-div{
                    width: auto;
                    height: initial;
                    border: 2px solid rgb(8, 177, 50);
                    margin: 20px;
                }
            </style>
        </head>
        <body>
            <h1>CSS Height Width property</h1>
            <div class="parent-div">
                <div class="child-div">
                      <p>Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipisicing elit. Nulla, in?</p>
                </div>
            </div>
        </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ---
        
        ### **CSS max-width and min-width Property:**
        
        CSS **`max-width`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`min-width`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Website ‡¶è Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Maximum ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Minimum Width Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ Normally ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Static Width ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ Window Size ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á Width ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ì‡¶á Width ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞  Window Size ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø window ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Scrollbar Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ Width Adjustment ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé Static ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶á Element ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Dynamic ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶¨‡¶æ Responsive(‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Device ‡¶è‡¶∞ Screen Size ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ Width Adjustment ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ) ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶á **`max-width`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`min-width`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶á Property ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Image ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ Element ‡¶è‡•§  Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
          <head>
            <style>
              .container{
                width: 800px;
                margin: 0 auto;
              }
              
              .container img{
                width: 100%;
              }
            </style>
          </head>
          <body>
            <div class="container">
              <img src="desk.png" alt="Desk Image">
              <article>
                <p>
                  Lorem ipsum dolor, sit amet consectetur adipisicing elit. Ipsam, sit pariatur placeat voluptatibus totam necessitatibus laborum repudiandae voluptas doloribus? Fugit adipisci magni laboriosam sint possimus! Lorem ipsum dolor, sit amet consectetur adipisicing elit. Ipsam, sit pariatur placeat voluptatibus totam necessitatibus laborum repudiandae voluptas doloribus? Fugit adipisci magni laboriosam sint possimus!
                </p>
              </article>
            </div>
          </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ **`div`** ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ Class Name ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø Container. ‡¶è‡¶á Container ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Image ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Text ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶á Container ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width `800px` Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Code ‡¶ü‡¶ø Run ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Browser ‡¶è ‡¶ó‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá Keyboard ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá **`Ctrl+Shift+C`** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá Developer Tools Open ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶õ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡•§
        
        ![Developers Tool.png](./document-Images/Developers_Tool.png)
        
        ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ Developers Tools Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßü  **`Ctrl+Shift+M`** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá Responsive Mode Open ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶õ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡•§
        
        ![Responsive Mode.png](./document-Images/Responsive_Mode.png)
        
        ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶æ Screen Width ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Mouse ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ Width Static ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Width ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ‡¶§‡ßá **`max-width`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`min-width`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
          <head>
            <style>
              .container{
                max-width: 800px;
                min-width: 300px;
                margin: 0 auto;
              }
              
              .container img{
              width: 100%;
              }
            </style>
          </head>
          <body>
            <div class="container">
              <img src="desk.png" alt="Desk Image">
              <article>
                <p>
                  Lorem ipsum dolor, sit amet consectetur adipisicing elit. Ipsam, sit pariatur placeat voluptatibus totam necessitatibus laborum repudiandae voluptas doloribus? Fugit adipisci magni laboriosam sint possimus! Lorem ipsum dolor, sit amet consectetur adipisicing elit. Ipsam, sit pariatur placeat voluptatibus totam necessitatibus laborum repudiandae voluptas doloribus? Fugit adipisci magni laboriosam sint possimus!
                </p>
              </article>
            </div>
          </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **`max-width`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ Window Width ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßá Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ Window Width ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width, Window ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá Adjustment ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé Responsive ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßü ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á Window Width ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü  Width ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`min-width`** Property ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ Example ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Min-width Value `300px` Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡¶≤ Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ Window ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width `300px` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Scrollbar Add ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
        
        ---
        
        ### **CSS max-height and min-height Property:**
        
        CSS **`max-height`** and **`min-height`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Maximum ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Minimum Height Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ `min-height` `100px` Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶á Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Content ‡¶è‡¶∞ Height ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ì ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ì Minimum Height `100px` ‡¶á ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
            <head>
            <style>
              *{
                margin: 0;
                padding: 0;
              }
              .container{
                max-width:500px;
                border:1px solid blue;
                margin: 10px auto;
                padding: 5px;
                min-height:100px;
              }
          </style>
            </head>
            <body>
              <h1>The min-height Property</h1>
              <div class="container">
                  <p> Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit.</p>
              </div>
            </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Content ‡¶è‡¶∞ Height ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® **`min-height`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Effects ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® Content ‡¶è‡¶∞ Height Minimum Height ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡ßú‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® Container ‡¶è‡¶∞ Height Automatic ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Content ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html

            <head>

                  margin: 0;
                  padding: 0;
                }

                  max-width:500px;

                  margin: 10px auto;
                  padding: 5px;
                  min-height:100px;
              }
            </style>
            </head>
            <body>
            <h1>The min-height Property</h1>
            <div class="container">
              <p> Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit.        > üí° Note: **`min-height`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá, **`height`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ **`height`** Property **`min-height`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ Effect ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
        ```
        
        **`min-height`** Property Value ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá (length, percentage(%), initial, inherit) ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡•§
        
        ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ **`max-height`** **`100px`** Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Content ‡¶è‡¶∞ Height **`max-height`** ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡ßú‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ Overflow ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
            <head>
            <style>
              *{
                margin: 0;
                padding: 0;
              }
              .container{
                max-width:500px;
                border:2px solid blue;
                margin: 10px auto;
                padding: 5px;
                max-height:100px;
              }
            </style>
            </head>
            <body>
            <h1>The max-height Property</h1>
              <div class="container">
                <p> Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. </p>
                <p> Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. </p>
                <p> Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. </p>
              </div>
            </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Container ‡¶è‡¶∞ Overflowing Content Handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ CSS **`overflow`** Property ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
            <head>
            <style>
              *{
                margin: 0;
                padding: 0;
              }
              .container{
                max-width:500px;
                border:2px solid blue;
                margin: 10px auto;
                padding: 5px;
                max-height:100px;
                overflow: auto;
              }
            </style>
            </head>
            <body>
            <h1>The max-height and overflow Property</h1>
            <div class="container">
              <p> Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. </p>
              <p> Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. </p>
              <p> Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. </p>
            </div>
            </body>
        ```

        ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá Content ‡¶è‡¶∞ Height ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Maximum Height ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Effects ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
        
         **`max-height`** Property Value ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá (none, length, percentage(%), initial, inherit) ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡•§
        
        ---
        
        ### CSS Overflow Property:
        
        CSS **`overflow`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Container ‡¶è‡¶∞ Content Overflow ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø Single Element ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Rectangular Box ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ CSS ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Box ‡¶è‡¶∞ Height Set ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ Height Content ‡¶è‡¶∞ Height ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Box ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ Height Or Width ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Content ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá Fit ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá! ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ Content ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Box ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ Overflow ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Problem ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø CSS **`overflow`** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ 
        
        CSS **`overflow`** Properties ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡ßá Value ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤:
        
        - **visible** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ By default ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Content ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Box ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
        - **hidden** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ Box ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ Content ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Overflow Content ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
        - **scroll** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ Box ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ Content ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ  Scrollbars Add ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ Scroll ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ Content ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
        - **auto** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ Scroll ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá  ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ Scrollbars ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® Add ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
        
        Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
            <head>
            <style>
              *{
                margin: 0;
                padding: 0;
              }
              .container{
                max-width:500px;
                border:2px solid blue;
                margin: 10px auto;
                padding: 5px;
                max-height:100px;
                overflow: hidden;
              }
            </style>
            </head>
            <body>
            <h1>The overflow Property</h1>
            <div class="container">
              <p style="color: blue"> Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. </p>
              <p style="color: green"> Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. </p>
              <p style="color: orange"> Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. </p>
            </div>
            </body>
        </html>
        ```
       > üí° Note: CSS `overflow` Property ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Block Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Height ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§

        ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`overflow-x`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`overflow-y`** Properties ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Horizontally ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Vertically ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ Both ‡¶è‡¶∞ Overflow Of Content Controll ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
            <head>
            <style>
              *{
                margin: 0;
                padding: 0;
              }
              .container{
                max-width:500px;
                border:2px solid blue;
                margin: 10px auto;
                padding: 5px;
                max-height:100px;
                overflow-y: scroll;
                overflow-x: auto;
              }
            </style>
            </head>
            <body>
            <h1>The overflow-x and overflow-y Property</h1>
            <div class="container">
              <p style="color: blue"> Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. </p>
              <p style="color: green"> Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. </p>
              <p style="color: orange"> Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. </p>
            </div>
            </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá Content ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Long Word ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá Browser Lines Break ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ Container ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
            <head>
            <style>
              *{
                margin: 0;
                padding: 0;
              }
              .container{
                width:200px;
                border:2px solid blue;
                margin: 10px auto;
                padding: 5px;
                max-height:100px;
              }
            </style>
            </head>
            <body>
            <h1>The overflow-wrap Property</h1>
            <div class="container">
              <p style="color: blue"> Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semperrrrrrrrrrrrrrrrrrrrrrrrrrdaddadaadaaaadar diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. </p>
            </div>
            </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`overflow-wrap`** ‡¶è‡¶á Property ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
        
        CSS **`overflow-wrap`** Properties ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨:
        
        - **normal** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ By Default ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Long Word Break ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
        - **anywhere** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® Long Words Overflow ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® Long Words ‡¶ï‡ßá Break ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
        - **break-word** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® Long Words Overflow ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® Long Words ‡¶ï‡ßá Break ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
        - **initial** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá Value ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Default Value.
        - **inherit** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Parent Value ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
        
        Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
            <head>
            <style>
              div {
                width: 150px; 
                border: 1px solid black;
              }
              
              div.a {
                overflow-wrap: normal;
              }
              
              div.b {
                overflow-wrap: break-word;
              }
              
              div.c {
                overflow-wrap: anywhere;
              }
            </style>
            </head>
            <body>
            <h1>The overflow-wrap Property</h1>
            
            <h2>overflow-wrap: normal (default):</h2>
            <div class="a">This div contains a very long word: thisisaveryveryveryveryveryverylongword. The long word will not break and wrap to the next line.</div>
            
            <h2>overflow-wrap: break-word:</h2>
            <div class="b">This div contains a very long word: thisisaveryveryveryveryveryverylongword. The long word will break and wrap to the next line.</div>
            
            <h2>overflow-wrap: anywhere:</h2>
            <div class="c">This div contains a very long word: thisisaveryveryveryveryveryverylongword. The long word will break and wrap to the next line.</div>
            </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ---
        
    - ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® CSS Box Sizing Property ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á‡•§
        
        CSS **box-sizing** Property ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ Style Property ‡¶Ø‡¶æ HTML Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Box Model ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Box Model ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á Structure ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Size ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá padding border  ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç margin ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
        Box Sizing Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶ø Value ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡¶É
        
        - **content-box(default)** ‚Üí width ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç height ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ Content ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü, padding ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç border ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡•§
        - **border-box** ‚Üí width ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç height Content , padding ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç border ‡¶∏‡¶π ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
        
        ### **content-box(default):**
        
        ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® **`box-sizing: content-box;`** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Height ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ Content ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ padding, border ‡¶¨‡¶æ margin ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø padding ‡¶¨‡¶æ border ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßÉ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html lang="en">
          <head>
            <style>
              .content-box-example {
                width: 200px;
                height: 100px;
                padding: 20px;
                border: 5px solid black;
                box-sizing: content-box;
                background-color: lightblue;
              }
            </style>
          </head>
          <body>
            <div class="content-box-example">Content Box Example</div>
          </body>
        </html>
        
        ```
        
        ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, **`.content-box-example`** class ‡¶è‡¶∞ **width** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **height** ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ Content ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§ padding (20px) ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç border (5px) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá:
        
        - ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü Width = 200px (width) + 20px (padding left) + 20px(padding  right) + 5px(border left) + 5px(border right) = 250px.
        - ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü Height = 100px (height) + 20px (padding top) + 20px(padding  bottom) + 5px(border top) + 5px(border bottom) = 150px.
        
        ### **border-box:**
        
        ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® **`box-sizing: border-box;`** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Height **content**, **padding** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **border** ‡¶∏‡¶π ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé padding ‡¶¨‡¶æ border ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html lang="en">
          <head>
            <style>
              .border-box-example {
                width: 200px;
                height: 100px;
                padding: 20px;
                border: 5px solid black;
                box-sizing: border-box;
                background-color: lightgreen;
              }
            </style>
          </head>
          <body>
            <div class="border-box-example">Border Box Example</div>
          </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
        ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, **`.border-box-example`** ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∞ **width** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **height** ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá **padding** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **border** ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á, ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá:
        
        - ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü Width = 200px.
        - ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü Height= 100px .
        
        ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® **padding** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **border** ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ì Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü **Width** ‡¶¨‡¶æ **Height** ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé, Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Content ‡¶è‡¶∞ Size ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá **padding** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **border** ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
        
        ‡¶è‡¶á Property ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Design ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Layout ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Developer Universal selector ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á Property ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá‡¶á Declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá Website ‡¶è‡¶∞ Layout Structure ‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ 
        
        ### ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨:
        
        - **content-box**: ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Content ‡¶è‡¶∞ Size ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **padding** ‡¶¨‡¶æ **border** ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶á ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
        - **border-box**: ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **padding** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **border** ‡¶∏‡¶π ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
        
    ---
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á CSS Text Formatting Properties ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
    
    **CSS Text Formatting Properties** ‡¶π‡¶≤ CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Text Display ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Property ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ Size, Color, Font ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø Customize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá CSS Text Formatting Properties ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶∏‡¶π ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤:
    CSS Text Formatting Properties ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶¨‡•§
    
    - Text Properties.
    - Font Properties.
    
    ### CSS Text Properties:
    
    CSS Text Properties ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡¶É color, text-align, direction, vertical-align, text-decoration, text-transform, text-indent, letter-spacing, line-height, word-spacing, white-space, text-shadow. ****‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶∏‡¶π ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶¨‡•§ **** 
    
    ### CSS Text Color:
    
    CSS **`color`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ Color Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ CSS Color ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Color ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Build-in Color, HEX, HSL, RGB ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
        <style>
          .build-in{
            color: red;
          }
          
          .hex{
            color: #ff0000;
          }
          
          .hsl{
            color: hsl(0,100%,50%);
          }
          
          .rgb{
            color: rgb(255,0,0);
          }
        </style>
        </head>
        <body>
        <h1 class="build-in">This Color is set with Build-in Color</h1>
        <h1 class="hex">This Color is set with HEX value</h1>
        <h1 class="hsl">This Color is set with HSL Value</h1>
        <h1 class="rgb">This Color is set with RGB Value</h1>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
     ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`color`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá **`background-color`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
        <style>
          .build-in{
            color: black;
            background-color: skyblue;
          }
          
          .hex{
            color: #000000;
            background-color:#ee82ee;
          }
          
          .hsl{
            color: hsl(0,0%,100%);
            background-color: hsl(147, 50%, 47%);
          }
          
          .rgb{
            color: rgb(255,255,255);
            background-color: rgb(255, 99, 71)
          }
        </style>
        </head>
        <body>
        <h1 class="build-in">This Color is set with Build-in Color</h1>
        <h1 class="hex">This Color is set with HEX value</h1>
        <h1 class="hsl">This Color is set with HSL Value</h1>
        <h1 class="rgb">This Color is set with RGB Value</h1>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ### CSS Text Alignment:
    
    CSS **`text-align`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Horizontally Text Alignment Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ CSS **`text-align`** Property ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Value ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤:
    
    - **left** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ By Default ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Text ‡¶ï‡ßá Container ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
    - **right** ‚Üí Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Text ‡¶ï‡ßá Container ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
    - **center** ‚Üí Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Text ‡¶ï‡ßá Container ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
    - **justify** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Text ‡¶ï‡ßá Container ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® Width ‡¶è ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá Text ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßá‡•§
    
    Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
        <style>
          h1 {
            text-align: center;
          }
          
          h2 {
            text-align: left;
          }
          
          h3 {
            text-align: right;
          }
          p {
            text-align: justify;
          }
        </style>
        </head>
        <body>
        <h1>Heading 1 (center)</h1>
        <h2>Heading 2 (left)</h2>
        <h3>Heading 3 (right)</h3>
        <p>Lorem ipsum dolor, sit amet consectetur adipisicing elit. Ipsam, sit pariatur placeat voluptatibus totam necessitatibus laborum repudiandae voluptas doloribus? Fugit adipisci magni laboriosam sint possimus! Lorem ipsum dolor, sit amet consectetur adipisicing elit. Ipsam, sit pariatur placeat voluptatibus totam necessitatibus laborum repudiandae voluptas doloribus? Fugit adipisci magni laboriosam sint possimus!</p>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`text-align-last`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ Last Line ‡¶è‡¶∞ Alignment ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
        <style>
          p.a {
            text-align-last: right;
          }
          
          p.b {
            text-align-last: center;
          }
          
          p.c {
            text-align-last: justify;
          }
        </style>
        </head>
        <body>
        <h1>The text-align-last Property</h1>
        
        <h2>text-align-last: right:</h2>
        <p class="a">Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. Vestibulum volutpat tellus diam, consequat gravida libero rhoncus ut.</p>
        
        <h2>text-align-last: center:</h2>
        <p class="b">Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. Vestibulum volutpat tellus diam, consequat gravida libero rhoncus ut.</p>
        
        <h2>text-align-last: justify:</h2>
        <p class="c">Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Etiam semper diam at erat pulvinar, at pulvinar felis blandit. Vestibulum volutpat tellus diam, consequat gravida libero rhoncus ut.</p>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```

    ### CSS Text Direction:
    
    CSS **`direction`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`unicode-bidi`** Properties ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Text Direction Change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
            <style>
          p.ex1 {
            direction: rtl;
            unicode-bidi: bidi-override;
          }
            </style>
        </head>
        <body>
        <p>This is the default text direction.</p>
        <p class="ex1">This is right-to-left text direction.</p>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
