    ### **CSS Vertical Alignment:**
    
    CSS **`vertical-align`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Vertically Alignment Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example: 
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
        <style>
          img.a {
            vertical-align: baseline;
          }
          
          img.b {
            vertical-align: text-top;
          }
          
          img.c {
            vertical-align: text-bottom;
          }
          
          img.d {
            vertical-align: sub;
          }
          
          img.e {
            vertical-align: super;
          }
        </style>
        </head>
        <body>
        <h1>The vertical-align Property</h1>
        
        <h2>vertical-align: baseline (default):</h2>
        <p>An <img class="a" src="sqpurple.gif" width="9" height="9"> image with a default alignment.</p> 
        
        <h2>vertical-align: text-top:</h2>
        <p>An <img class="b" src="sqpurple.gif" width="9" height="9"> image with a text-top alignment.</p> 
        
        <h2>vertical-align: text-bottom:</h2>
        <p>An <img class="c" src="sqpurple.gif" width="9" height="9"> image with a text-bottom alignment.</p>
        
        <h2>vertical-align: sub:</h2>
        <p>An <img class="d" src="sqpurple.gif" width="9" height="9"> image with a sub alignment.</p> 
        
        <h2>vertical-align: sup:</h2>
        <p>An <img class="e" src="sqpurple.gif" width="9" height="9"> image with a super alignment.</p>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ### CSS Text Decoration:
    
    CSS **`text-decoration-line`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ Decoration Line(‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ **`text-decoration-line`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡¶É
    
    - **overline** ‚Üí Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá Line ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
    - **line-through** ‚Üí  Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Line ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
    - **underline** ‚Üí Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá Line ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
    
    Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
        <style>
          h1 {
            text-decoration-line: overline;
          }
          
          h2 {
            text-decoration-line: line-through;
          }
          
          h3 {
            text-decoration-line: underline;
          }
        </style>
        </head>
        <body>
        <h1>Overline text decoration</h1>
        <h2>Line-through text decoration</h2>
        <h3>Underline text decoration</h3>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ Value ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
        <style>
          p.ex {
            text-decoration-line: overline underline;
          }
        </style>
        </head>
        <body>
          <p class="ex">Overline and underline text decoration.</p>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`text-decoration-color`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`text-decoration-style`** properties ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ Decoration Color ‡¶ì Style ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ **`text-decoration-style`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ solid, double, dotted, dashed, wavy ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example: 
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
        <style>
          h1 {
            text-decoration-line: underline;
            text-decoration-style: solid; /* this is default */
            text-decoration-color: blue;
          }
          
          h2 {
            text-decoration-line: underline;
            text-decoration-style: double;
              text-decoration-color: green;
          }
          
          h3 {
            text-decoration-line: underline;
            text-decoration-style: dotted;  
          }
          
          p.ex1 {
            text-decoration-line: underline;
            text-decoration-style: dashed;  
          }
          
          p.ex2 {
            text-decoration-line: underline;
            text-decoration-style: wavy;  
          }
          
          p.ex3 {
            text-decoration-line: underline;
            text-decoration-color: red;  
            text-decoration-style: wavy;  
          }
        </style>
        </head>
        <body>
          <h1>Heading 1</h1>
          <h2>Heading 2</h2>
          <h3>Heading 3</h3>
          <p class="ex1">A paragraph.</p>
          <p class="ex2">Another paragraph.</p>
          <p class="ex3">Another paragraph.</p>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ **`text-decoration-thickness`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Decoration Line ‡¶è‡¶∞ Thickness Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example: 
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
        <style>
          h1 {
            text-decoration-line: underline;
            text-decoration-thickness: auto;  /* this is default */
          }
          
          h2 {
            text-decoration-line: underline;
            text-decoration-thickness: 5px;
          }
          
          h3 {
            text-decoration-line: underline;
            text-decoration-thickness: 25%;
          }
          
          p {
            text-decoration-line: underline;
            text-decoration-color: red;  
            text-decoration-style: double;
            text-decoration-thickness: 5px;  
          }
        </style>
        </head>
        <body>
          <h1>Heading 1</h1>
          <h2>Heading 2</h2>
          <h3>Heading 3</h3>
          <p>A paragraph.</p>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Shorthand Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Property ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    
    **CSS Text Decoration Shorthand Property Syntax**: `**text-decoration:  text-decoration-line¬†(required)  text-decoration-color¬†(optional)  text-decoration-style¬†(optional)  text-decoration-thickness¬†(optional)**`
    
    Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
        <style>
          h1 {
            text-decoration: underline;
          }
          
          h2 {
            text-decoration: underline red;
          }
          
          h3 {
            text-decoration: underline red double;
          }
          
          p {
            text-decoration: underline red double 5px;
          }
        </style>
        </head>
        <body>
          <h1>Heading 1</h1>
          <h2>Heading 2</h2>
          <h3>Heading 3</h3>
          <p>A paragraph.</p>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ### CSS Text Transformation:
    
    CSS **`text-transform`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ Letters ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Uppercase ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Lowercase ‡¶è Transform ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ Example: 
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
        <style>
          h2.uppercase {
            text-transform: uppercase;
          }
          
          h2.lowercase {
            text-transform: lowercase;
          }
          
          h2.capitalize {
            text-transform: capitalize;
          }
        </style>
        </head>
        <body>
          <h1>Using the text-transform property</h1>
          
          <h2 class="uppercase">This text is transformed to uppercase.</h2>
          <h2 class="lowercase">This text is transformed to lowercase.</h2>
          <h2 class="capitalize">This text is capitalized.</h2>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ### CSS Text Spacing Properties:
    
    CSS Text Spacing Properties ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤:
    
    - **text-indent** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ First Line ‡¶è‡¶∞ Indentation ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
    - **letter-spacing** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø Letter ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡ßá Space ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
    - **line-height** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ Line Height ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ By Default Paragraph ‡¶è‡¶∞ Line Height 18px ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
    - **word-spacing** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ Word ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡ßá Space ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
    - **white-space** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Text Wrapping ‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
    
    Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
            <style>
              p.A {
                text-indent: 50px;
              }
              p.B {
                letter-spacing: 15px;
              }
              p.C {
                line-height: 50px;
              }
              p.D {
                word-spacing: 50px;
              }
              p.E {
                white-space: nowrap;
              }
            </style>
        </head>
        <body>
          <h1>Using text-indent</h1>
          
          <p class="A">Lorem ipsum dolor, sit amet consectetur adipisicing elit. Ipsam, sit pariatur placeat voluptatibus totam necessitatibus laborum repudiandae voluptas doloribus? Fugit adipisci magni laboriosam sint possimus! Lorem ipsum dolor, sit amet consectetur adipisicing elit.</p>
          
          <h1>Using letter-spacing</h1>
          
          <p class="B">Lorem ipsum dolor, sit amet consectetur adipisicing elit. Ipsam, sit pariatur placeat voluptatibus totam necessitatibus laborum repudiandae voluptas doloribus? Fugit adipisci magni laboriosam sint possimus! Lorem ipsum dolor, sit amet consectetur adipisicing elit.</p>
          
          <h1>Using line-height</h1>
          
          <p class="C">Lorem ipsum dolor, sit amet consectetur adipisicing elit. Ipsam, sit pariatur placeat voluptatibus totam necessitatibus laborum repudiandae voluptas doloribus? Fugit adipisci magni laboriosam sint possimus! Lorem ipsum dolor, sit amet consectetur adipisicing elit.</p>
          
          <h1>Using word-spacing</h1>
          
          <p class="D">Lorem ipsum dolor, sit amet consectetur adipisicing elit. Ipsam, sit pariatur placeat voluptatibus totam necessitatibus laborum repudiandae voluptas doloribus? Fugit adipisci magni laboriosam sint possimus! Lorem ipsum dolor, sit amet consectetur adipisicing elit.</p>
          
          <h1>Using white-space</h1>
          
          <p class="E">Lorem ipsum dolor, sit amet consectetur adipisicing elit. Ipsam, sit pariatur placeat voluptatibus totam necessitatibus laborum repudiandae voluptas doloribus? Fugit adipisci magni laboriosam sint possimus! Lorem ipsum dolor, sit amet consectetur adipisicing elit.</p>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ### **CSS Text Shadow:**
    
    CSS **`text-shadow`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Shadow Effect ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ 
    
    **CSS Text Shadow Property Value Syntax**: **`text-shadow: horizontal-shadow vertical-shadow blur-effect shadow-color`**  
    
    Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
            <style>
              h1 {
                text-shadow: 2px 2px ;
              }
              h2 {
                text-shadow: 2px 5px red;
              }
              h3 {
                text-shadow: 2px 2px 10px;
              }
              h4 {
                text-shadow: 2px 2px 10px red;
              }
            </style>
        </head>
        <body>
          <h1>Text-shadow effect!</h1>
          
          <h2>Text-shadow effect!</h2>
          
          <h3>Text-shadow effect!</h3>
          
          <h4>Text-shadow effect!</h4>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    More Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
        <head>
        <style>
          h1.A {
            color: white;
            text-shadow: 2px 2px 4px #000000;
          }
          h1.B {
            text-shadow: 0 0 3px #ff0000;
          }
          h1.C {
            text-shadow: 0 0 3px #ff0000, 0 0 5px #0000ff;
          }
          h1.D {
            color: white;
            text-shadow: 1px 1px 2px black, 0 0 25px blue, 0 0 5px darkblue;
          }
        </style>
        </head>
        <body>
          <h1 class="A">Text-shadow effect!</h1>
          <h1 class="B">Text-shadow effect!</h1>
          <h1 class="C">Text-shadow effect!</h1>
          <h1 class="D">Text-shadow effect!</h1>
        </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ### CSS Font Properties:
    
    CSS Font Properties ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡¶É font-family, font-size, font-style, font-variant, font, font-weight. ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶∏‡¶π ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶¨‡•§
    
    ### CSS Fonts:
    
    Website ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Font Choose ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ú‡¶® User Website Visit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ User Experience ‡¶è ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ Impact ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶∏‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï Font ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ö‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Brand ‡¶è‡¶∞ Strong Identity ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶∂‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Text ‡¶™‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® Font ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Font, Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Website ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü Font ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø Font Color ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Text Size ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ 
    
    ---
    
    ### CSS Font-Family Property:
    
    CSS **`font-family`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Website ‡¶è List of Font Families Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Text Content ‡¶è‡¶∞ Font-Face ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Property, Fallback System ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Multiple Font Name ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Font Browser Support ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Website ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ Windows Operating System ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`font-family: arial`** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Website Android Operating System ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ì Run ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, MAC Operating System ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ì Run ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® MAC Operating System ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Browser ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø **`font-family: arial`** ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® Browser ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá? ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Arial ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø  **`font-family`** ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Group ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá Browser ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá Replace ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá Browser ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ Default Font ‡¶è Replace ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶∑‡¶£‡ßÄ‡ßü Website ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® **`font-family`** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ 
    
    CSS ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ Font-Family Names ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤:
    
    - **family-name** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Font-Family ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Courier, Arial, Times ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§
    - **generic-family** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø **`font-family`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ Group of Family Name  ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á **`font-family`** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá font-families group ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ó‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§ Fallback System ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø group ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ font-family ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ font ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ['Courier New', Courier, monospace], ['Times New Roman', Times, serif], [Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif] ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§
    
    CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡ß´‡¶ü‡¶ø Generic Font Families ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤: Serif, Sans-serif, Monospace, Cursive, Fantasy. ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶£‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡¶É
    
    1. **serif** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Printing Writing ‡¶è, Books Writing ‡¶è, magazines ‡¶è, newspapers ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á font-family ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤: Georgia, Garamond, Times New Roman, Minion ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§
    2. **sans-serif** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ modern, formal ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç simple style ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø generic family. ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Digital form of Text ‡¶è‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á font-family ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤: Arial, Calibri, Verdana, Futura, Lato etc.
    3. **cursive** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá brush ‡¶¨‡¶æ pen ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶æ handwriting text ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü invitation letter, informal messages ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á font-family ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤: Insolente, Corsiva, Flanella, Belluccia, Zapfino etc.
    4. **monospace** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü instructions, mailling address, typewritten text ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á font-family ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤: Monaco, SimSun, Courier, Consolas, Inconsolata ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§
    5. **fantasy** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Text ‡¶ï‡ßá Expressive, Decorative ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Impactful ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á font-family ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤: Impact, Copperplate, Cracked, Critter ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§
    
        ![Generic font family.png](./document-Images/Generic_font_family.png)
    
    CSS **`font-family`** Property values ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤:
    
    **family-name/generic-family** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá font-family Name Or Generic-Family Name ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
    
    **initial** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ Default Value ‡¶ï‡ßá Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
    
    **inherit** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Value ‡¶ï‡ßá Parent Element ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Inherit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
    
    Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
            body {
                font-family: "lucida handwriting";  /* font-family Name */
            }
            h1 {
                font-family: initial;
            }
          .container {
            width: 400px;
            margin: 0 auto;
            font-family: inherit;
          }
          .p1 {
            font-family: "Times New Roman", Times, serif;  /* geniric-family Name */
          }
    
          .p2 {
            font-family:  Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; /* geniric-family Name */
          }
    
          .p3 {
            font-family: "Lucida Console", "Courier New", monospace; /* geniric-family Name */
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h1>CSS font-family</h1> <hr>
          <p class="p1">This is a paragraph, shown in the Times New Roman font.</p>
          <p class="p2">This is a paragraph, shown in the Arial font.</p>
          <p class="p3">This is a paragraph, shown in the Lucida Console font.</p>
          <p>This is a paragraph, shown in the Parent font.</p>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Font ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ One Word ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶∂‡¶á Quotation Marks ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‚ÄúTimes New Roman‚Äù, "Lucida Console", "Courier New" ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§ 
    
    > üí° **_Note_:** Generic-Family ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá Font ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ Website ‡¶è Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ(,) ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
    
    ---
    
    ### CSS Web Safe Fonts:
    
    CSS Web Safe Fonts ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á Fonts ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Browser ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Device ‡¶è By Default Universally Installed ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ì 100% Safe Web Fonts ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá Fonts Properly Install ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ì ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Always Generic **`font-family`** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨ Backup Fonts ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```css
    p {
        font-family: Tahoma, Verdana, sans-serif;
    }
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ Font Types ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ Second ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Third Fonts ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Backup Fonts. ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá First Fonts ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ 
    
    HTML ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Best Web Fonts ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤: 
    
    - Arial (sans-serif)
    - Verdana (sans-serif)
    - Tahoma (sans-serif)
    - Trebuchet MS (sans-serif)
    - Times New Roman (serif)
    - Georgia (serif)
    - Garamond (serif)
    - Courier New (monospace)
    - Brush Script MT (cursive)
    
    > üí° **_Note_:**  ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü Website Publish ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ Fonts Family ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® Browser ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Device ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Display ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§
    
    ### Use Google Font:
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ HTML Standards Fonts ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, Google Fonts ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Google Fonts ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Website ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶∑‡¶£‡ßÄ‡ßü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Google Fonts ‡¶è 1000 ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø Fonts ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Free ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ Easily ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
    
    **Google Font ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶Æ‡¶É**
    
    ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá  [**Google-fonts**](https://fonts.google.com/) ‡¶è‡¶á Link ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á Font Website ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á Font ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ö‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ HTML **`<head>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Google Font ‡¶ü‡¶ø Link ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Link ‡¶è‡¶∞ **`rel`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ Type ‚Äústylesheet‚Äù ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ **`href`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Google Font ‡¶è‡¶∞ URL ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
    
    **Syntax**:
    
     `<link rel=‚Äùstylesheet‚Äù href=‚Äùhttps://fonts.googleapis.com/css?family=Font_Name‚Äù>`
    
    **`Font_Name`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ Font ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ CSS ‡¶è **`font-family`** ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶á Font ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Website ‡¶è ‚ÄúSofia‚Äù Font ‡¶ü‡¶ø Use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example: 
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css?family=Sofia"/>
        <style>
          body {
            font-family: "Sofia", sans-serif;
          }
          .container {
            width: 400px;
            margin: auto;
            font-size: x-large;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h1>Sofia Font</h1>
          <p>Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet.</p>
          <p>123456790</p>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ "Trirong‚Äù ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∞ Google Font ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css?family=Trirong"/>
        <style>
          body {
            font-family: "Trirong", serif;
          }
          .container {
            width: 400px;
            margin: auto;
            font-size: x-large;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h1>Trirong Font</h1>
          <p>Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet.</p>
          <p>123456790</p>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    > üí° **_Note_:** Website ‡¶è Font ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá Fallback System ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶∂‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Generic Font Family ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Google Font ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Generic Font Family(Like sarif or sans-sarif) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
    
    ---
    
    ### **Use Multiple Google Fonts:**
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Multiple Google Fonts ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá Pipe Character( | ) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css?family=Audiowide|Sofia|Trirong"/>
        <style>
          .container{
            width:500px;
            margin:auto;
          }
          h1.a {
            font-family: "Audiowide", sans-serif;
          }
    
          h1.b {
            font-family: "Sofia", sans-serif;
          }
    
          h1.c {
            font-family: "Trirong", serif;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h1 class="a">Audiowide Font</h1>
    
          <h1 class="b">Sofia Font</h1>
    
          <h1 class="c">Trirong Font</h1>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    > üí° **_Note_:** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï Google Fonts ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶∏‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ Google Font ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ Google Server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Website Slow ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

    ---
    
    ### **CSS¬†Great Font Pairings:**
    
    Font Pairing ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶§‡ßã‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï Font ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßå‡¶∂‡¶≤, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¶‡ßÉ‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶∏‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï Font Pairing ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Design ‡¶ï‡ßá Professional ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶°‡¶º‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
    
    ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤ Design ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Great Font Pairings ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡•§ Font Pairing ‡¶è‡¶∞  ‡ß™‡¶ü‡¶æ Basic Rules ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤:
    
    - Complement ‚Üí ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® Font ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶¶ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Difference ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® Font.
    - Use Font Superfamilies ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Font Superfamily ‡¶π‡¶≤ Font ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ç, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á Superfamily ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶´‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶¶‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Lusida Superfamily ‡¶è‡¶∞ Fonts ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá : Lucida Sans, Lucida Serif, Lucida Typewriter Sans, Lucida Typewriter Serif and Lucida Math.
    - Contrast is king ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ú‡¶®‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶§‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶´‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶§ Contrast ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Font Pairing ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø Font ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßÉ‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    - Choose Only One Boss ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶§‡¶ø Font Pairing ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã, Design ‡¶¨‡¶æ Typography ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Font Pairing (‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶´‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶£) ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ö‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
    
    ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Popular Font Pairings ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤ : 
    
    1. **Georgia and Verdana**
    
        Georgia and Verdana ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Classic Combination. ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ Web Safe Font Standards ‡¶ì ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
          <head>
            <style>
              body {
                font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;
                font-size: 16px;
              }
              .container {
                width: 600px;
                margin: auto;
              }
        
              h1 {
                font-family: Georgia, serif;
                font-size: 46px;
              }
            </style>
          </head>
          <body>
            <div class="container">
              <h1>Beautiful Norway</h1>
              <p>
                Norway has a total area of 385,252 square kilometers and a population of 5,438,657 (December 2020). Norway is bordered by Sweden, Finland and Russia to the north-east, and the Skagerrak to the south, with Denmark on the other side.
              </p>
              <p>
                Norway has beautiful mountains, glaciers and stunning fjords. Oslo, the capital, is a city of green spaces and museums. Bergen, with colorful wooden houses, is the starting point for cruises to the dramatic Sognefjord. Norway is also known for fishing, hiking and skiing.
              </p>
            </div>
          </body>
        </html>
        ```
    
    2. **Helvetica and Garamond**
    
        Helvetica and Garamond ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Classic Combination. ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ Web Safe Font Standards ‡¶ì ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
          <head>
            <style>
              body {
                font-family: Garamond, serif;
                font-size: 16px;
              }
              .container {
                width: 600px;
                margin: auto;
              }
        
              h1 {
                font-family: Helvetica, sans-serif;
                font-size: 46px;
              }
            </style>
          </head>
          <body>
            <div class="container">
              <h1>Beautiful Norway</h1>
              <p>
                Norway has a total area of 385,252 square kilometers and a population of 5,438,657 (December 2020). Norway is bordered by Sweden, Finland and Russia to the north-east, and the Skagerrak to the south, with Denmark on the other side.
              </p>
              <p>
                Norway has beautiful mountains, glaciers and stunning fjords. Oslo, the capital, is a city of green spaces and museums. Bergen, with colorful wooden houses, is the starting point for cruises to the dramatic Sognefjord. Norway is also known for fishing, hiking and skiing.
              </p>
            </div>
          </body>
        </html>
        ```
    
    **Popular Google Font Pairings:**
    
    ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Popular Google Font Pairings ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤ : 
    
    1. **Merriweather and Open Sans**
    
        Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
          <head>
            <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css?family=Merriweather|Open+Sans">
            <style>
              body {
                font-family: "Open Sans", sans-serif;
                font-size: 16px;
              }
              .container {
                width: 600px;
                margin: auto;
              }
        
              h1 {
                font-family: Merriweather, serif;
                font-size: 46px;
              }
            </style>
          </head>
          <body>
            <div class="container">
              <h1>Beautiful Norway</h1>
              <p>
                Norway has a total area of 385,252 square kilometers and a population of 5,438,657 (December 2020). Norway is bordered by Sweden, Finland and Russia to the north-east, and the Skagerrak to the south, with Denmark on the other side.
              </p>
              <p>
                Norway has beautiful mountains, glaciers and stunning fjords. Oslo, the capital, is a city of green spaces and museums. Bergen, with colorful wooden houses, is the starting point for cruises to the dramatic Sognefjord. Norway is also known for fishing, hiking and skiing.
              </p>
            </div>
          </body>
        </html>
        ```
    
    1. **Ubuntu and Lora**
    
        Example: 
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
          <head>
            <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css?family=Ubuntu|Lora">
            <style>
              body {
                font-family: Lora, serif;
                font-size: 16px;
              }
              .container {
                width: 600px;
                margin: auto;
              }
        
              h1 {
                font-family: Ubuntu, sans-serif;
                font-size: 46px;
              }
            </style>
          </head>
          <body>
            <div class="container">
              <h1>Beautiful Norway</h1>
              <p>
                Norway has a total area of 385,252 square kilometers and a population of 5,438,657 (December 2020). Norway is bordered by Sweden, Finland and Russia to the north-east, and the Skagerrak to the south, with Denmark on the other side.
              </p>
              <p>
                Norway has beautiful mountains, glaciers and stunning fjords. Oslo, the capital, is a city of green spaces and museums. Bergen, with colorful wooden houses, is the starting point for cruises to the dramatic Sognefjord. Norway is also known for fishing, hiking and skiing.
              </p>
            </div>
          </body>
        </html>
        ```
    
    3. **Abril Fatface and Poppins**
    
        Example:
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
          <head>
            <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css?family=Abril+Fatface|Poppins">
            <style>
              body {
                font-family: Poppins, sans-serif;
                font-size: 16px;
              }
              .container {
                width: 600px;
                margin: auto;
              }
        
              h1 {
                font-family: 'Abril Fatface', serif;
                font-size: 46px;
              }
            </style>
          </head>
          <body>
            <div class="container">
              <h1>Beautiful Norway</h1>
              <p>
                Norway has a total area of 385,252 square kilometers and a population of 5,438,657 (December 2020). Norway is bordered by Sweden, Finland and Russia to the north-east, and the Skagerrak to the south, with Denmark on the other side.
              </p>
              <p>
                Norway has beautiful mountains, glaciers and stunning fjords. Oslo, the capital, is a city of green spaces and museums. Bergen, with colorful wooden houses, is the starting point for cruises to the dramatic Sognefjord. Norway is also known for fishing, hiking and skiing.
              </p>
            </div>
          </body>
        </html>
        ```

        > ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì Google Fonts ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶ú‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á [Link](https://www.w3schools.com/howto/howto_google_fonts.asp) ‡¶¨‡¶æ [Google Font](https://fonts.google.com/) ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    
        ### **@font-face Properties**
    
        `@font-face` CSS rule ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ CSS rule ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ú‡ßá custom fonts ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø font ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá Webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶õ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡ßÄ fonts ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶®‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ê font ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì‡•§`@font-face` CSS rule ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø font ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá Custom font ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶Æ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶∏‡¶π ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡¶É
        
        @font-face {
        
        font-family: family name(‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡•§);
        
        src: url(desktop folder url) format(‚Äôformat Name‚Äô);
        
        ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá font related ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø properties ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ì ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ 
        
        }
    
        Example: 
        
        ```css
        /*Custom font declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡¶ø*/
        @font-face {
            font-family: 'MyCustomFont';
            src: url('fonts/mycustomfont.woff2') format('woff2'),
                url('fonts/mycustomfont.woff') format('woff');
            font-weight: normal;
            font-style: normal;
        }
        
        /*Custom font ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡¶ø*/
        body {
            font-family: 'MyCustomFont', sans-serif;
        }
        ```
        
        ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ `MyCustomFont` ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø custom font ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ `src` ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá font ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ path ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø (`mycustomfont.woff2` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `mycustomfont.woff`), ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá font ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ `font-family` ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ body ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á font ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡•§ 
    
        ### ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü?
        
        1. **Custom Font ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ**: ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶´‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶®‡•§ `@font-face` ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ custom fonts ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡•§
        2. **‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá font Install ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá fallback ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ**: ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü font ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá `@font-face` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü font ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶®‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
        3. **Font Customization**: Font Size, Structure, ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶∑‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡ßÄ‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Unique ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
        
        ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ç, ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶†‡¶®‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶æ, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§
        
        ### ‡¶∏‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶§‡¶æ:
        
        1. **Performance**: Custom Font ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶æ Website ‡¶è‡¶∞ Loading Time ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá font ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Download ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
        2. **‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ ‡¶Ö‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶§‡¶æ**: Font File ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Load ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá, Webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ Loading ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü font rendering ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®, Font ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ Default Font ‡¶è Switch ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ)‡•§
        
    ---
    
    ### CSS Font Style:
    
    CSS **`font-style`** Property Mostly ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Italic Text Style ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Property ‡¶§‡ßá normal, italic, oblique ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶æ Value ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ Italic ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Oblique Value ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ **`font-family`** ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá **`italic`** Value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Italic ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ , ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá **`oblique`** Value ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü‡¶ï‡¶•‡¶æ Normally Italic ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá **`italic`** Value ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ Forcefully Italic ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá **`oblique`** Value ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§   Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 400px;
            margin: 0 auto;
            font-family: Georgia, "Times New Roman", Times, serif;
          }
          p.normal {
            font-style: normal;
          }
    
          p.italic {
            font-style: italic;
          }
    
          p.oblique {
            font-style: oblique;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h1>The font-style property</h1>
          <hr />
          <p class="normal">This is a paragraph in normal style.</p>
          <p class="italic">This is a paragraph in italic style.</p>
          <p class="oblique">This is a paragraph in oblique style.</p>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### CSS Font Weight Property:
    
    CSS **`font-weight`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Font ‡¶è‡¶∞ Weight ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Font ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ **`font-weight`** Property ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Value ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤: normal, lighter, bold, bolder, initial, inherit. ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ **`font-weight`** Property ‡¶§‡ßá(100-900) Value use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá (100-300) ‚Üí Lighter Value, (400) ‚Üí Normal Value, (500-700) ‚Üí Bold Value, (700-900) ‚Üí Bolder Value. Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 400px;
            margin: 0 auto;
            font-family: "Segoe UI", Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif;
          }
          p.normal {
            font-weight: normal;
          }
    
          p.light {
            font-weight: lighter;
          }
    
          p.thick {
            font-weight: bold;
          }
    
          p.thicker {
            font-weight: 900; /*bolder value*/
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h1>The font-weight property</h1>
          <hr />
          <p class="normal">This is a paragraph.</p>
          <p class="light">This is a paragraph.</p>
          <p class="thick">This is a paragraph.</p>
          <p class="thicker">This is a paragraph.</p>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ### CSS Font Variant Property:
    
    CSS **`font-variant`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Text ‡¶ï‡ßá Small-Caps(‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü Size ‡¶è‡¶∞ Capital Latter) Font ‡¶è Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ normal, small-caps, inherit, Value ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 400px;
            margin: 0 auto;
          }
          h2.normal {
            font-variant: normal;
          }
    
          h2.small {
            font-variant: small-caps;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h1>The font-variant property</h1>
          <hr />
          <h2 class="normal">My name is Hege Refsnes.</h2>
          <h2 class="small">My name is Hege Refsnes.</h2>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ### CSS Font Size Property:
    
    CSS **`font-size`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ Height ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Font Size Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ By Default Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ **`font-size`** 16px ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ **`font-size`** Property ‡¶§‡ßá Basic ‡¶Ø‡ßá Value ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤:  xx-small(9px), x-small(10px), small(13.3px), smaller(14px), medium(16px), large(18px), larger(19px), x-large(24px), xx-large(32px). Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: 0 auto;
          }
          p.A {
            font-size: xx-small;
          }
          p.B {
            font-size: x-small;
          }
          p.C {
            font-size: small;
          }
          p.D {
            font-size: smaller;
          }
          p.E {
            font-size: medium;
          }
          p.F {
            font-size: large;
          }
          p.G {
            font-size: larger;
          }
          p.H {
            font-size: x-large;
          }
          p.I {
            font-size: xx-large;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h1>CSS font-size Property</h1>
          <hr />
          <p class="A">This paragraph font-size value is xx-small.</p>
          <p class="B">This paragraph font-size value is x-small.</p>
          <p class="C">This paragraph font-size value is small.</p>
          <p class="D">This paragraph font-size value is smaller.</p>
          <p class="E">This paragraph font-size value is madium.</p>
          <p class="F">This paragraph font-size value is large.</p>
          <p class="G">This paragraph font-size value is larger.</p>
          <p class="H">This paragraph font-size value is x-large.</p>
          <p class="I">This paragraph font-size value is xx-large.</p>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    Web Design ‡¶è Font ‡¶è‡¶∞ Size Manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á Important. ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Website ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ  Base Font Size Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ 16px ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 18px ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ Heading ‡¶è‡¶∞ Size, ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ Size ‡¶è‡¶∞ 2 ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶£ ‡¶¨‡¶æ  1.5 ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶£ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá  Website Text ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ Font Size ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá 9px ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ì ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Website ‡¶è (read more button Text) ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Text ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá Minimum Size 9px ‡¶π‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§
    
    CSS **`font-size`** Property Absolute or Relative ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ 
    
    - **Absolute size** ‚Üí  ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Size Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ Text Size, User Change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ Absolute Size ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Output ‡¶è‡¶∞ Psychical Size ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Pixel ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Font size Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§
    - **Relative size** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ Size ‡¶Ü‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∞ Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Size ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶®‡•§ Relative Size ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ Text Size User Change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Percentage ‡¶¨‡¶æ em Property value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Font size Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§
    

    > üí° Note: Normally ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Font ‡¶è‡¶∞ Default Size ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá 16px Or 1em(16px=1em).

    
    ---
    
    ### **Set Font Size with Pixels:**
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Pixel ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶ì **`font-size`** Property Value ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§  Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 400px;
            margin: 0 auto;
          }
          h1 {
            font-size: 50px;
          }
    
          h2 {
            font-size: 30px;
          }
    
          p {
            font-size: 12px;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h1>This is heading 1</h1>
          <h2>This is heading 2</h2>
          <p>This is a paragraph.</p>
          <p>This is another paragraph.</p>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ### **Set Font Size with Percentage(%):**
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Percentage(%) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶ì **`font-size`** Property Value ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Parent Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Font Size ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Value Add ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 600px;
            margin: 0 auto;
            font-size: 18px;
          }
          h1.A{
            font-size: 200%;
          }
    
          h2.B {
            font-size: 100%;
            
          }
    
          p {
            font-size: 100%;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h1 class="A">This is heading 1</h1>
          <h2 class="B">This is heading 2</h2>
          <p>This is a paragraph.</p>
          <p>This is another paragraph.</p>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ### **Set Font Size With Em**
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Font Size **`em`** Unit ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶ì Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Text ‡¶ï‡ßá Resize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ Parent Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Font Size ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Value Add ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï developer pixels ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßá **`em`** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶õ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ Default Font Size ‡¶π‡¶≤ 16px Or 1em. Pixels ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá **`em`** ‡¶è Size Calculate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ Formula ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá: $pixels/16 = em$. Example: 
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          h1 {
            font-size: 2.5em; /* 40px/16=2.5em */
          }
          
          h2 {
            font-size: 1.875em; /* 30px/16=1.875em */
          }
          
          p {
            font-size: 0.875em; /* 14px/16=0.875em */
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <h1>This is heading 1</h1>
        <h2>This is heading 2</h2>
        <p>This is a paragraph.</p>
        <p>Specifying the font-size in em allows all major browsers to resize the text.
        Unfortunately, there is still a problem with older versions of IE. When resizing the text, it becomes larger/smaller than it should.</p>
        
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    > üí° **_Note_**: ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Font Size ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Pixel, Percentage(%), Em. ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨? ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Website ‡¶è‡¶∞ Font Size Change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ Fixed ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Pixel(px) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Website Font ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ‡ßü  Auto ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ Device Width ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé Responsive ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    
    ---
    
    ### **Use a Combination of Percent and Em:**
    
    ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï Old Version Browser ‡¶è Font Size ‡¶¨‡ßú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßú ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá Percent(%) ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`em`**  Combination ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Font-Size Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Body ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Default **`font-size`** Percent(%) ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          body {
            font-size: 100%;
          }
          
          h1 {
            font-size: 2.5em;
          }
          
          h2 {
            font-size: 1.875em;
          }
          
          p {
            font-size: 0.875em;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <h1>This is heading 1</h1>
        <h2>This is heading 2</h2>
        <p>This is a paragraph.</p>
        <p>Specifying the font-size in percent and em displays the same size in all major browsers, and allows all browsers to resize the text! </p>
      
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ### Responsive Font Size:
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ Size `vw` Unit ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‚Äúviewport width‚Äù ‡¶è set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Viewport ‡¶π‡¶≤ Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ Window ‡¶è‡¶∞ Size.  
    
    **1vw = 1% of viewport width.**
    
    Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
      <body>
        <h1 style="font-size: 5vw">Responsive Text</h1>
    
        <p style="font-size: 3vw">
          Resize the browser window to see how the text size scales.
        </p>
    
        <p style="font-size: 3vw">
          Use the "vw" unit when sizing the text. 5vw will set the size to 5% of the viewport width.
        </p>
    
        <p>
          Viewport is the browser window size. 1vw = 1% of viewport width. If the viewport is 50cm wide, 1vw is 0.5cm.
        </p>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    > üí° Note: ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø viewport ‡¶è‡¶∞ size 50cm ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∂‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá 1vw = 0.5cm.

    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ Size `vh` Unit ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‚Äúviewport height‚Äù ‡¶è set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    
    **1vh = 1% of viewport height.**
    
    Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
      <body>
        <h1 style="font-size: 5vh">Responsive Text</h1>
    
        <p style="font-size: 3vh">
          Resize the browser window to see how the text size scales.
        </p>
    
        <p style="font-size: 3vh">
          Use the "vh" unit when sizing the text. 5vh will set the size to 5% of the viewport height.
        </p>
    
        <p>
          Viewport is the browser window size. 1vh = 1% of viewport height. If the viewport is 50cm high, 1vh is 0.5cm.
        </p>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ### CSS Font Shorthand Property:
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`font`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá CSS Font Shorthand Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    
    **CSS Font Property Shorthand Syntax**: **`font: font-style font-variant font-weight font-size(required)/line-height font-family(required)`**
    
    Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 600px;
            margin: auto;
          }
          p.a {
            font: 20px Arial, sans-serif;     /* font-size, font-family*/
          }
    
          p.b {
            font: italic small-caps bold 12px/30px Georgia, serif;  /*font-style font-variant font-weight font-size(required)/line-height font-family(required)*/
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h1>The font Property</h1>
    
          <p class="a">
            This is a paragraph. The font size is set to 20 pixels, and the font family is Arial.
          </p>
    
          <p class="b">
            This is a paragraph. The font is set to italic, small-caps and bold, the font size is set to 12 pixels, the line height is set to 30 pixels, and the font family is Georgia.
          </p>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á HTML File ‡¶è CSS Icons ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨?
    
    CSS Icon ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Program ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø File ‡¶è‡¶∞ Small Graphical Representation. ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Image ‡¶¨‡¶æ Symbol ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ HTML Page ‡¶è Icon ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá Icon Library ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Icon ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á HTML Page ‡¶è Icon ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Icons ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Format ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Icons ‡¶è‡¶∞ color, shadow, size ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    
    **Font Awesome Icons:**
    
    ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Font Awesome Icon Library ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Font Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶¨‡•§ Font Awesome Library ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Download ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á‡•§ 
    
    Font Awesome 5 ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá [**fontawsome.com**](http://fontawsome.com) ‡¶è ‡¶ó‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Account ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Account ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Kit-Code ‡¶∏‡¶π Link ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Link ‡¶ü‡¶ø HTML **`<head>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ 
    
    **`<script src="https://kit.fontawesome.com/yourcode.js" crossorigin="anonymous"></script>`**
    
    ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® HTML Element(like **`<i>`** or **`<span>`** ) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü  Icon Name, Class ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <title>Font Awesome Icons</title>
        <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1" />
        <script src="https://kit.fontawesome.com/cb8340b770.js" crossorigin="anonymous"></script>
        <!--Get your own code at fontawesome.com-->
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h1>Font Awesome icon library</h1>
    
          <p>Some Font Awesome icons:</p>
          <i class="fa fa-cloud"></i>
          <i class="fa fa-heart"></i>
          <i class="fa fa-car"></i>
          <i class="fa fa-file"></i>
          <i class="fa fa-bars"></i>
    
          <p>Styled Font Awesome icons (size and color):</p>
          <i class="fa fa-cloud" style="font-size: 24px"></i>
          <i class="fa fa-cloud" style="font-size: 36px"></i>
          <i class="fa fa-cloud" style="font-size: 48px; color: red"></i>
          <i class="fa fa-cloud" style="font-size: 60px; color: lightblue"></i>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Font Awesome 4 Library ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ CDN Link ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ó‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á CDN Link ‡¶ü‡¶ø HTML **`<head>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
    
    **`<link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/4.7.0/css/font-awesome.min.css">`**
    
    ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® HTML Element(like **`<i>`** or **`<span>`** ) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü  Icon Name, Class ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <title>Font Awesome Icons</title>
        <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1" />
        <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/4.7.0/css/font-awesome.min.css">  
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h1>Font Awesome icon library</h1>
    
          <p>Some Font Awesome icons:</p>
          <i class="fa fa-cloud"></i>
          <i class="fa fa-heart"></i>
          <i class="fa fa-car"></i>
          <i class="fa fa-file"></i>
          <i class="fa fa-bars"></i>
    
          <p>Styled Font Awesome icons (size and color):</p>
          <i class="fa fa-cloud" style="font-size: 24px"></i>
          <i class="fa fa-cloud" style="font-size: 36px"></i>
          <i class="fa fa-cloud" style="font-size: 48px; color: red"></i>
          <i class="fa fa-cloud" style="font-size: 60px; color: lightblue"></i>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    **Bootstrap Icons:**
    
    ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Bootstrap Glyphicons Library ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Font Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶¨‡•§ Bootstrap Glyphicons Library ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Download ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ CDN Link ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ó‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á CDN Link ‡¶ü‡¶ø HTML **`<head>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
    
    **`<link rel="stylesheet" href="[https://maxcdn.bootstrapcdn.com/bootstrap/3.3.7/css/bootstrap.min.css](https://maxcdn.bootstrapcdn.com/bootstrap/3.3.7/css/bootstrap.min.css)">`**
    
    ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® HTML Element(like **`<i>`** or **`<span>`** ) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü  Icon Name, Class ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <title>Font Awesome Icons</title>
        <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1" />
        <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://maxcdn.bootstrapcdn.com/bootstrap/3.3.7/css/bootstrap.min.css"> 
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h1>Bootstrap icon library</h1>
    
          <p>Some Bootstrap icons:</p>
          <i class="glyphicon glyphicon-cloud"></i>
          <i class="glyphicon glyphicon-remove"></i>
          <i class="glyphicon glyphicon-user"></i>
          <i class="glyphicon glyphicon-envelope"></i>
          <i class="glyphicon glyphicon-thumbs-up"></i>
          <br><br>
    
          <p>Styled Bootstrap icons (size and color):</p>
          <i class="glyphicon glyphicon-cloud" style="font-size:24px;"></i>
          <i class="glyphicon glyphicon-cloud" style="font-size:36px;"></i>
          <i class="glyphicon glyphicon-cloud" style="font-size:48px;color:red;"></i>
          <i class="glyphicon glyphicon-cloud" style="font-size:60px;color:lightblue;"></i>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    **Google Icons:**
    
    ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Google Material Icon Library ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Font Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶¨‡•§ Google Material Icon Library ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Download ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ CDN Link ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ó‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á CDN Link ‡¶ü‡¶ø HTML **`<head>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
    
    **`<link rel="stylesheet" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/icon?family=Material+Icons">`**
    
    ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® HTML Element(like **`<i>`** or **`<span>`** ) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü  Icon Name, Class ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <title>Font Awesome Icons</title>
        <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1" />
        <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/icon?family=Material+Icons">
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h1>Google icon library</h1>
    
          <p>Some Google icons:</p>
          <i class="material-icons">cloud</i>
          <i class="material-icons">favorite</i>
          <i class="material-icons">attachment</i>
          <i class="material-icons">computer</i>
          <i class="material-icons">traffic</i>
          <br><br>
    
          <p>Styled Google icons (size and color):</p>
          <i class="material-icons" style="font-size:24px;">cloud</i>
          <i class="material-icons" style="font-size:36px;">cloud</i>
          <i class="material-icons" style="font-size:48px;color:red;">cloud</i>
          <i class="material-icons" style="font-size:60px;color:lightblue;">cloud</i>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
