- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á CSS Links Property State ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø?
    
    CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá HTML Link ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® Style ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ HTML Link ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ State ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Style ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø HTML Link ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡ß™‡¶ü‡¶ø State ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤:
    
    - **a:link** ‚Üí  ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Unvisited Normal Link ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
    - **a:visited** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ User Link ‡¶ü‡¶ø Visit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
    - **a:hover** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ User Link ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ Mouse Hover ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
    - **a:active** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Link Clicked ‡¶π‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
    
    Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
          /* unvisited link */
          a:link {
            color: red;
          }
    
          /* visited link */
          a:visited {
            color: green;
          }
    
          /* mouse over link */
          a:hover {
            color: hotpink;
          }
    
          /* selected link */
          a:active {
            color: blue;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h2>Styling a link depending on state</h2>
          <p>
            <b><a href="https://www.google.com/" target="_blank">This is a link</a></b>
          </p>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    > üí° **_Note_:** Link State Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Order Rules ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® **`a:hover`** ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶∂‡¶á **`a:link`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`a:visited`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ **`a:active`** ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶∂‡¶á **`a:hover`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

    
    CSS **`text-decoration`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value **`none`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Link ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ Underline ‡¶ü‡¶æ Remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example: 
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
          /* unvisited link */
          a:link {
            text-decoration: none;
          }
    
          /* visited link */
          a:visited {
            text-decoration: none;
          }
    
          /* mouse over link */
          a:hover {
            text-decoration: underline;
          }
    
          /* selected link */
          a:active {
            text-decoration: underline;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h2>Styling a link with text-decoration property</h2>
          <p><b><a href="https://www.google.com/" target="_blank">This is a link</a></b></p>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    CSS **`background`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Link ‡¶è‡¶∞ Background Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
          /* unvisited link */
          a:link {
            text-decoration: none;
            background-color: yellow;
          }
    
          /* visited link */
          a:visited {
            text-decoration: none;
            background-color: cyan;
          }
    
          /* mouse over link */
          a:hover {
            text-decoration: underline;
            background-color: lightgreen;
          }
    
          /* selected link */
          a:active {
            text-decoration: underline;
            background-color: hotpink;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h2>Styling a link with text-decoration and background-color property</h2>
          <p><b><a href="https://www.google.com/" target="_blank">This is a link</a></b></p>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Link ‡¶ï‡ßá CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶Æ‡ßá Button Style ‡¶è Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
          .button{
            margin-bottom: 20px;
          }
          /* unvisited link and visited link*/
          .button a:link, .button a:visited {
            background-color: #f1493d;
            color: white;
            padding: 14px 24px;
            text-align: center;
            text-decoration: none;
          }
    
          /* mouse over link and selected link*/
          .button a:hover, .button a:active{
            background-color: red;
          }
    
          .button1 a:link, .button1 a:visited {
            background-color: white;
            color: black;
            border: 2px solid green;
            border-radius: 10px;
            padding: 10px 20px;
            text-align: center;
            text-decoration: none;
          }
    
          .button1 a:hover, .button1 a:active {
            background-color: green;
            color: white;
          }
    
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h2>Styling a link Like a Button</h2>
          <p class="button"><b><a href="https://www.google.com/" target="_blank">This is a link</a></b></p>
           <hr>
          <p class="button1"><b><a href="https://www.google.com/" target="_blank">This is a another link</a></b></p>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ CSS **`cursor`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Website ‡¶è‡¶∞ Cursor Icon, Change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h2>The cursor Property</h2>
    
          <p>Mouse over the words to change the cursor.</p>
          <span style="cursor:auto">auto</span><br>
          <span style="cursor:crosshair">crosshair</span><br>
          <span style="cursor:default">default</span><br>
          <span style="cursor:e-resize">e-resize</span><br>
          <span style="cursor:help">help</span><br>
          <span style="cursor:move">move</span><br>
          <span style="cursor:n-resize">n-resize</span><br>
          <span style="cursor:ne-resize">ne-resize</span><br>
          <span style="cursor:nw-resize">nw-resize</span><br>
          <span style="cursor:pointer">pointer</span><br>
          <span style="cursor:progress">progress</span><br>
          <span style="cursor:s-resize">s-resize</span><br>
          <span style="cursor:se-resize">se-resize</span><br>
          <span style="cursor:sw-resize">sw-resize</span><br>
          <span style="cursor:text">text</span><br>
          <span style="cursor:w-resize">w-resize</span><br>
          <span style="cursor:wait">wait</span><br>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á CSS List Properties ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø?
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ CSS Properties ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá HTML List ‡¶ï‡ßá Style ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ 
    
    CSS **`list-style-type`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá List Item ‡¶è‡¶∞ Marker Type Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ CSS **`list-style-type`** Value ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤: circle, square, decimal, decimal-leading-zero, lower-alpha, lower-roman, upper-alpha, upper-roman ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§ Example
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
          ul.a {
            list-style-type: circle;
          }
    
          ul.b {
            list-style-type: square;
          }
    
          ol.c {
            list-style-type: upper-roman;
          }
    
          ol.d {
            list-style-type: lower-alpha;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h2>The list-style-type Property</h2>
    
            <p>Example of unordered lists:</p>
            <ul class="a">
              <li>Coffee</li>
              <li>Tea</li>
              <li>Coca Cola</li>
            </ul>
    
            <ul class="b">
              <li>Coffee</li>
              <li>Tea</li>
              <li>Coca Cola</li>
            </ul>
    
            <p>Example of ordered lists:</p>
            <ol class="c">
              <li>Coffee</li>
              <li>Tea</li>
              <li>Coca Cola</li>
            </ol>
    
            <ol class="d">
              <li>Coffee</li>
              <li>Tea</li>
              <li>Coca Cola</li>
            </ol>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    CSS **`list-style-type`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value **`none`** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü List Marker Type ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
          ul.a {
            list-style-type: none;
          }
    
          ol.b {
            list-style-type: none;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h2>The list-style-type Property</h2>
    
            <p>Example of unordered lists:</p>
            <ul class="a">
              <li>Coffee</li>
              <li>Tea</li>
              <li>Coca Cola</li>
            </ul>
    
            <p>Example of ordered lists:</p>
            <ol class="b">
              <li>Coffee</li>
              <li>Tea</li>
              <li>Coca Cola</li>
            </ol>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    CSS **`list-style-image`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü List Item Marker ‡¶è Image ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
          ul {
            list-style-image: url('sqpurple.gif');
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h2>The list-style-image Property</h2>
    
          <p>The list-style-image property specifies an image as the list item marker:</p>
    
          <ul>
            <li>Coffee</li>
            <li>Tea</li>
            <li>Coca Cola</li>
          </ul>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    CSS **`list-style-position`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá List Item Markers(bullet points) ‡¶è‡¶∞ Position ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ CSS **`list-style-position`** Property Value ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá: outside, inside. Example: 
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
          ul.a {
            list-style-position: outside;
            
          }
          ul.a li{
            border: 1px solid black;
          }
    
          ul.b {
            list-style-position: inside;
          }
          ul.b li{
            border: 1px solid black;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h1>The list-style-position Property</h1>
    
          <h2>list-style-position: outside (default):</h2>
          <ul class="a">
            <li>Coffee - A brewed drink prepared from roasted coffee beans, which are the seeds of berries from the Coffea plant</li>
            <li>Tea - An aromatic beverage commonly prepared by pouring hot or boiling water over cured leaves of the Camellia sinensis, an evergreen shrub (bush) native to Asia</li>
            <li>Coca Cola - A carbonated soft drink produced by The Coca-Cola Company. The drink's name refers to two of its original ingredients, which were kola nuts (a source of caffeine) and coca leaves</li>
          </ul>
    
          <h2>list-style-position: inside:</h2>
          <ul class="b">
            <li>Coffee - A brewed drink prepared from roasted coffee beans, which are the seeds of berries from the Coffea plant</li>
            <li>Tea - An aromatic beverage commonly prepared by pouring hot or boiling water over cured leaves of the Camellia sinensis, an evergreen shrub (bush) native to Asia</li>
            <li>Coca Cola - A carbonated soft drink produced by The Coca-Cola Company. The drink's name refers to two of its original ingredients, which were kola nuts (a source of caffeine) and coca leaves</li>
          </ul>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    **Remove Default Settings:**
    
    List ‡¶è‡¶∞ Default Setting Remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá Marker /Bullets ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ Default Padding ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Margin Remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
          ul.demo {
            list-style-type: none;
            margin: 0;
            padding: 0;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <p>Default list:</p>
          <ul>
            <li>Coffee</li>
            <li>Tea</li>
            <li>Coca Cola</li>
          </ul>
    
          <p>Remove bullets, margin and padding from list:</p>
          <ul class="demo">
            <li>Coffee</li>
            <li>Tea</li>
            <li>Coca Cola</li>
          </ul>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### **List - Shorthand property**
    
    CSS **`list-style`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example: 
    
    **Syntax**: **`list-style: list-style-type list-style-position list-style-image`**
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
          ul {
            list-style: square inside url("sqpurple.gif");
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h2>The list-style Property</h2>
    
          <p>The list-style property is a shorthand property, which is used to set all the list properties in one declaration.</p>
    
          <ul>
            <li>Coffee</li>
            <li>Tea</li>
            <li>Coca Cola</li>
          </ul>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    **Styling List With Colors:**
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá List ‡¶ï‡ßá Color ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ List ‡¶è‡¶∞ Look ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï Interesting ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
          ol {
            background: #ff9999;
            padding: 20px;
          }
    
          ul {
            background: #3399ff;
            padding: 20px;
          }
    
          ol li {
            background: #ffe5e5;
            color: darkred;
            padding: 5px;
            margin-left: 35px;
          }
    
          ul li {
            background: #cce5ff;
            color: darkblue;
            margin: 5px;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h1>Styling Lists With Colors</h1>
    
          <ol>
            <li>Coffee</li>
            <li>Tea</li>
            <li>Coca Cola</li>
          </ol>
    
          <ul>
            <li>Coffee</li>
            <li>Tea</li>
            <li>Coca Cola</li>
          </ul>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á CSS Table ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Style ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü?
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá HTML Table ‡¶ï‡ßá Style ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ HTML Table ‡¶è‡¶∞ Better Look ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ CSS ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡•§
    
    **CSS Table Border:**
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ CSS **`border`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Table ‡¶è‡¶∞ Border Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Table ‡¶è‡¶∞ Border ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø **`table, th, td`** Selector ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **`border`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
          table, th, td {
            border: 1px solid;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h2>Add a border to a table:</h2>
    
          <table>
            <tr>
              <th>Firstname</th>
              <th>Lastname</th>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Ahamed</td>
              <td>Khan</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Jabedul</td>
              <td>Islam</td>
            </tr>
          </table>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    **CSS Table Width and Height:**
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Table ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Height Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
          table, th, td {
            border: 1px solid;
          }
          table {
            width: 100%;
            height: 100px;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h2>Add a Full width to a table:</h2>
    
          <table>
            <tr>
              <th>Firstname</th>
              <th>Lastname</th>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Ahamed</td>
              <td>Khan</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Jabedul</td>
              <td>Islam</td>
            </tr>
          </table>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`th`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`td`** ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Height Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
          table, th, td {
            border: 1px solid;
          }
          table {
            width: 100%;
            height: 100px;
          }
          th{
            height:50px;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h2>Add a Full width to a table:</h2>
    
          <table>
            <tr>
              <th>Firstname</th>
              <th>Lastname</th>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Ahamed</td>
              <td>Khan</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Jabedul</td>
              <td>Islam</td>
            </tr>
          </table>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    **CSS Table Border Collapse:**
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≤‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¨ Table ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá Double Border ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ Table , Table Heading ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Table Data ‡¶è‡¶∞ Separate Border ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ CSS **`border-collapse`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Table Border ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Single Border ‡¶è ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
          table, th, td {
            border: 1px solid;
          }
          table {
            width: 100%;
            border-collapse: collapse;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h2>Let the table borders collapse</h2>
    
          <table>
            <tr>
              <th>Firstname</th>
              <th>Lastname</th>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Ahmed</td>
              <td>Khan</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Jabedul</td>
              <td>Islam</td>
            </tr>
          </table>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    **CSS Table Alignment**:
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Table ‡¶è‡¶∞ Text ‡¶ï‡ßá Horizontally ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Vertically ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Alignment Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ CSS **`text-align`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Table ‡¶è‡¶∞ Text ‡¶ï‡ßá Horizontally(left, right or center) Align ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ By Default Text, Left Alignment ‡¶è ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
          table, th, td {
            border: 1px solid;
          }
          table {
            width: 100%;
            height: 100px;
            text-align: center;
                    border-collapse: collapse;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h2>The text-align Property</h2>
    
          <table>
            <tr>
              <th>Firstname</th>
              <th>Lastname</th>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Ahamed</td>
              <td>Khan</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Jabedul</td>
              <td>Islam</td>
            </tr>
          </table>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ CSS **`vertical-align`** Property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Vertically(like top, bottom or middle Alignment Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ By Default ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Middle ‡¶è ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
          table, th, td {
            border: 1px solid;
          }
          table {
            width: 100%;
            height: 150px;
            border-collapse: collapse;
          }
          td{
            vertical-align: bottom;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h2>The vertical-align Property</h2>
    
          <table>
            <tr>
              <th>Firstname</th>
              <th>Lastname</th>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Ahamed</td>
              <td>Khan</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Jabedul</td>
              <td>Islam</td>
            </tr>
          </table>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    **CSS Table Padding:**
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ CSS Padding Property **`<th>`** and **`<td>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Table ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì Better ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
          table, td, th {  
            border: 1px solid #ddd;
            text-align: left;
          }
    
          table {
            border-collapse: collapse;
            width: 100%;
          }
    
          th, td {
            padding: 15px;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h2>The padding Property</h2>
    
          <p>This property adds space between the border and the content in a table.</p>
          
          <table>
            <tr>
              <th>Firstname</th>
              <th>Lastname</th>
              <th>Savings</th>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Peter</td>
              <td>Griffin</td>
              <td>$100</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Lois</td>
              <td>Griffin</td>
              <td>$150</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Joe</td>
              <td>Swanson</td>
              <td>$300</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Cleveland</td>
              <td>Brown</td>
              <td>$250</td>
            </tr>
          </table>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    **CSS Horizontal Dividers:**
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`border-bottom`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá **`<th>`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`<td>`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Horizontal Dividers Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
          table {
            border-collapse: collapse;
            width: 100%;
          }
    
          th, td {
            padding: 10px;
            text-align: left;
            border-bottom: 1px solid #ddd;
           
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h2>Bordered Table Dividers</h2>
          <p>Add the border-bottom property to th and td for horizontal dividers:</p>
          
          <table>
            <tr>
              <th>Firstname</th>
              <th>Lastname</th>
              <th>Savings</th>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Peter</td>
              <td>Griffin</td>
              <td>$100</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Lois</td>
              <td>Griffin</td>
              <td>$150</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Joe</td>
              <td>Swanson</td>
              <td>$300</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Cleveland</td>
              <td>Brown</td>
              <td>$250</td>
            </tr>
          </table>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    **CSS Hoverable Table:**
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`<tr>`** Element ‡¶è `:hover` Selector ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Table Rows ‡¶ï‡ßá Highlight ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:

    ```html
              <th>Firstname</th>
              <th>Lastname</th>
    ```

    **CSS Striped Tables**:
    
    Striped Tables ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø **`nth-child()`** Selector ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`odd`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`even`** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
          table {
            border-collapse: collapse;
            width: 100%;
          }
    
          th, td {
            padding: 10px;
            text-align: left;
           
          }
          tr:nth-child(odd){background-color:rgb(247, 232, 184);}
          tr:nth-child(even) {background-color:rgb(255, 241, 224);}
          tr:hover {background-color: rgb(221, 167, 96); color: white}
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h2>Striped Table</h2>
          <hr>
          <p>For zebra-striped tables, use the nth-child() selector and add a background-color to all even (or odd) table rows:</p>
          
          <table>
            <tr>
              <th>Firstname</th>
              <th>Lastname</th>
              <th>Savings</th>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Sopon</td>
              <td>islam</td>
              <td>$100</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Lois</td>
              <td>Griffin</td>
              <td>$150</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Joe</td>
              <td>Swanson</td>
              <td>$300</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Cleveland</td>
              <td>Brown</td>
              <td>$250</td>
            </tr>
          </table>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    **CSS Table Color:**
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Table ‡¶è CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® Color ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Table ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶∑‡¶£‡ßÄ‡ßü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:

    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>

      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;

          tr:nth-child(even) {background-color:rgb(255, 241, 224);}
          
          tr:hover {background-color: rgb(236, 196, 142); color: white}
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h2>Colored Table Header</h2>
          
          <table>
            <tr>
              <th>Firstname</th>
              <th>Lastname</th>
              <th>Savings</th>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Peter</td>
              <td>Griffin</td>
              <td>$100</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Lois</td>
              <td>Griffin</td>
              <td>$150</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Joe</td>
              <td>Swanson</td>
              <td>$300</td>

              <td>Brown</td>
              <td>$250</td>
            </tr>
          </table>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    **CSS caption-side Property:**
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`caption-side`** Property ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Table Caption ‡¶è‡¶∞ Placement ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .container {
            width: 500px;
            margin: auto;
          }
          .mytable1 {
            border-collapse: collapse;
            width: 100%;
            margin-bottom: 40px;
          }
    
          .mytable1  th, td {
            padding: 10px;
            text-align: left;
           
          }
          .mytable1  th{
            background-color: rgb(180, 164, 20);
            color:white;
          }
          .mytable1  tr:nth-child(odd){background-color:rgb(247, 232, 184);}
          .mytable1  tr:nth-child(even) {background-color:rgb(255, 241, 224);}
          
          .mytable1  tr:hover {background-color: rgb(236, 196, 142); color: white}
    
          .mytable2 {
            border-collapse: collapse;
            width: 100%;
            margin-bottom: 40px;
          }
    
           .mytable2{
            caption-side: bottom;
           }
          .mytable2  th, td {
            padding: 10px;
            text-align: left;
          }
          .mytable2  th{
            background-color: rgb(180, 164, 20);
            color:white;
          }
          .mytable2  tr:nth-child(odd){background-color:rgb(247, 232, 184);}
          .mytable2  tr:nth-child(even) {background-color:rgb(255, 241, 224);}
          
          .mytable2  tr:hover {background-color: rgb(236, 196, 142); color: white}
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div class="container">
          <h1>The caption-side Property</h1>
          <hr>
          <p>The caption-side property specifies the placement of a table caption:</p>
          <h2>caption-side: top (default):</h2>
          <table class="mytable1">
            <caption>Table 1.1</caption>
            <tr>
              <th>Firstname</th>
              <th>Lastname</th>
              <th>Savings</th>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Peter</td>
              <td>Griffin</td>
              <td>$100</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Lois</td>
              <td>Griffin</td>
              <td>$150</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Joe</td>
              <td>Swanson</td>
              <td>$300</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Cleveland</td>
              <td>Brown</td>
              <td>$250</td>
            </tr>
          </table>
    
          <h2>caption-side: bottom:</h2>
          <table class="mytable2">
            <caption>Table 1.1</caption>
            <tr>
              <th>Firstname</th>
              <th>Lastname</th>
              <th>Savings</th>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Peter</td>
              <td>Griffin</td>
              <td>$100</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Lois</td>
              <td>Griffin</td>
              <td>$150</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Joe</td>
              <td>Swanson</td>
              <td>$300</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
              <td>Cleveland</td>
              <td>Brown</td>
              <td>$250</td>
            </tr>
          </table>
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```

- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á CSS Display Property ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
    
    CSS display property ‡¶π‡¶≤ CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Website ‡¶è‡¶∞ Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Layout Control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßÉ‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá Default ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Display Value ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Website ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Element ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡ßü‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ Box ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ CSS Property ‡¶Ü‡ßü‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶á Box ‡¶è‡¶∞ Behavior ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ 
    
    CSS Display Property Value ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡¶É
    
    **inline** ‚áí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Block Element ‡¶ï‡ßá Inline Element ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ Inline Element ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ Content ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Inline Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá top ‡¶¨‡¶æ bottom ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã margin ‡¶¨‡¶æ padding ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶™‡ßú‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ (‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞)‡•§
    
    **block** ‚áí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Inline Element ‡¶ï‡ßá block ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Element ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ width ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶®‡ßá‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Width ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡•§
    
    **inline-block** ‚áí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Inline ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Block ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¨‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø Inline Element ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá Block Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ Width, Height, Margin, Padding ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
    
    **none** ‚áí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ Browser ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßÅ‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ 
    
    inherit ‚áí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Parent Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ display property ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ 
    
    ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ **`display: flex;`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`display: grid;`** property ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ö‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ 
    
    Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <style>
          .block {
            display: block;
            background: purple;
            color: white;
            padding: 12px;
          }
    
          .inline {
            display: inline;
            background: coral;
            color: white;
            padding: 12px;
          }
          .inline-block {
            display: inline-block;
            background: crimson;
            color: white;
            padding: 12px;
          }
          .none {
            display: none;
            background: green;
            color: white;
            padding: 12px;
          }
          .parent {
            display: block;
            background: deeppink;
            color: white;
            padding: 12px;
          }
    
          .inherit {
            display: inherit;
            background: white;
            color: black;
            padding: 5px;
          }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <span class="block">This is an inline element.</span> <!--‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Inline Element. -->
        <p class="inline">This is an block element.</p><br /> <!--‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Block Element. -->
        <p class="inline-block">This is an inline block element.</p>  <!--‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Block Element. -->
        <div class="none"> <!--‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Block Element. -->
          <p>Hello World</p>
        </div>
        <div class="parent">  <!--‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Block Element. -->
          <span class="inherit">This Element get his Parent Properties</span> <!--‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Inline Element. -->
        </div>
      </body>
    </html>
    
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá,
    
    - ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Inline Element ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá CSS Property `display:block`  ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Block Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
    - ‡ß®‡ßü Element ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Block Element ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá CSS Property `display:inline`  ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Inline Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ top ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç bottom ‡¶è‡¶∞ padding ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡ßü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶†‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
    - ‡ß©‡ßü Element ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Block Element ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá CSS Property `display:inline-block`  ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Inline ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Block ‡¶â‡¶≠‡ßü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ top ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç bottom ‡¶è‡¶∞ padding ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡ß®‡ßü ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶†‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
    - ‡ß™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• Element ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Block Element ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá CSS Property `display:none`  ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Browser ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
    - ‡ß´‡¶Æ Element ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Block Element‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Inline Element. ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶∞ CSS Property ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá `display:inherit;` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ Parent Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Property value ‡¶ï‡ßá Inherit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ Parent property value ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ block ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ì Block Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
    
    ---

    # ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®...

- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á HTML & CSS Project ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßü ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
    
    **Note:** Project ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶ö ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ font-family ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡•§ 
    
    Note: Website design ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶∂‡¶á Website ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá responsive ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé  Laptop, tablet, mobile device ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶® website ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá show ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá design ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§  Responsive ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶•‡¶æ :
    
    1. Desktop First Approach.
    2. Mobile First Approach. 
    
    **Desktop First Approach**: ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Desktop ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Design Ready ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Laptop, Tablet, Mobile Device ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Responsive ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Approach ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á Break point ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶§‡ßá Media Query ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡¶É
    
    - Desktop Device/Extra Large Device(width ‚â§ 1400px)
    - Laptop Device/Large Device(width ‚â§ 1200px)
    - Tablet Device/Medium Device(width ‚â§ 992px)
    - Mobile Device/Small Device(width ‚â§ 768px)
    - Mobile Device/Extra Small Device(width ‚â§ 576px)
    
    **Mobile First Approach**: ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Mobile ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Design Ready ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Tablet, Laptop, Desktop  Device ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Responsive ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡•§
    
    **Note**: Responsive ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á Head Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ Code ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡ßá Responsive Code ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì Responsiveness ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ 
    
    > <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    > 
    
    **SEO - CSS**: ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Design ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ Website ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá SEO Friendly ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤: 
    
    - Head tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá proper ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ title ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
    - Website ‡¶è‡¶∞ Proper Information ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá Meta Tag Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®  Meta Name.
    
      1. **author** ‚áí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ content ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá Website ‡¶è‡¶∞ Owner ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

      2. **description** ‚áí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ Content ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá Website ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Description ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Description ‡¶ü‡¶æ Google ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Website ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Google Search ‡¶è Show ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Website ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á Description ‡¶∏‡¶π Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ 

      3. **keywords** ‚áí  ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ Content ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Website ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßü‡ßá‡¶∞ Keywords ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§   

      4. **robots** ‚áí  ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Google BOT ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶á‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ Content ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á Links ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Follow ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ 
    
    - Proper Heading Tags ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® h1‚áí h2‚áí h3 ‚áí h4 ‡¶è‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§
    
    **CSS Performance and Optimization**: 
    
    - Image Optimization ‚áí  Website ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á Image ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á webp format ‡¶è ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ webp format ‡¶è Image ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Size ‡¶è ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Load ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§  ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Image Optimization ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
    
    ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Website ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ png/jpg/jpeg Image ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá webp format ‡¶è Convert ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ 
    
      ‡ßß. [https://squoosh.app/](https://squoosh.app/) 

      ‡ß®. [https://www.freeconvert.com/png-to-webp](https://www.freeconvert.com/png-to-webp)
